Current Commentary

Northwest Border Defense and Development of the Northwest 8

Before Huang Musong, the Central Government's Special Envoy, Took Office, Many Chinese People Had New Hopes for the Development of the Northwest. They Believed that Huang's Trip Would Eliminate Local Opinions and Bridge the Years of Division Between the Han and Hui People. Unexpectedly, Reality was the Opposite of Ideal. Huang's Group Stayed in Xinjiang for Less Than a Month. During Their Stay, There Was a Coup in Dihua. According to the General Press, This Coup Was Neither a Serious Escalation of Han-Hui Conflict nor Caused by Any Sudden Problem. It Was Purely Due to Technical Political Relations, Which Led to a Misunderstanding Between the Special Envoy and Local Officials. As a Result, All the Staff of the Special Envoy's Office Left Xinjiang. Special Envoy Huang Also Returned to Beijing Not Long Ago. According to the Central Government's Judgment and General Social Speculation, if the Government Appoints Liu Wenlong and Sheng Shicai to Lead Xinjiang Province, Then Everything Can Be Settled. At Least, Political Changes Will Not Be Expanded. Given Time, Things Can be Gradually Remedied. This View May Be Believable.

Although the Division Between the Han and Hui People in Xinjiang Province is Said to Be Difficult to Fundamentally Resolve, the Area is Vast, Accounting for Nearly Four-Tenths of the Eighteen Inland Provinces. Traffic is Obstructed. Only the Border Areas Adjacent to Other Countries such as Britain and Russia Have Some Trade. The General Economic Society is Backward, Still in the Transition Period from Pastoral to Rural Economy. Moreover, the Population is Sparse. Although Production is Abundant, the Mentality of Being Content with the Status Quo is Greater Than the Will to Make Progress. Therefore, Local Officials and Leaders of General Society Also Quietly Abide by the Old Habits of Decades Ago. In Politics, They Remotely Support the Central Government, but Locally, They Each Rule Their Own Territory. In Reality, There is No So-Called Active Ambition to Develop Elsewhere. They Only Seek to Maintain Their Current State and Preserve Their Existing Positions. This is Enough to Satisfy Them. This is Why Xinjiang Has Maintained its Original State for the Past Twenty-Two Years. It is Probably Also Due to the Terrain. However, After the European War, the World's Consumer Markets Shrank, and the Sources of Raw Materials Were Limited. Since the Economic Panic of 1929 Began, Capitalist Countries Have Actively Developed Markets. Xinjiang, a Plateau Area with Many Sandy Deserts, is Not Enough to Serve as a Market. However, It is Better Than Nothing. After the Soviet Revolution, It Was Initially Only a Socialist Experiment. In Practice, it Was Not Enough to Threaten Capitalist Countries. Therefore, Xinjiang's Position Several Years Ago Did Not Have as Serious a Political Nature as It Does Now. As for the So-Called Conspiracy to Establish a Hui State and the Plan to Divide Our Northwest, Individual Attempts May Have Existed. However, Public Advocacy Was Never Heard. Recently, the Soviet Union's Five-Year Plan Has Been Implemented. The Turkestan-Siberia Railway Has Been Completed. Central Asia is in Its Grasp. The Hui People of Xinjiang Have Naturally Felt Extremely Stimulated. Therefore, Britain, Which Rules India, Has Seized the Opportunity to Enter. First, to Prevent the Expansion of Hui Influence. Second, to Prevent the Extension of Soviet Influence. Third, to Expand the Market to Facilitate the Development of Trade. At the Same Time, After Plundering the Four Northeastern Provinces, Japan is Taking Further Steps to Fully Realize Its So-Called Continental Policy, Intending to Invade Inner Mongolia. Therefore, the Number of Japanese Spies Sneaking Into Xinjiang Recently Has Reached No Less Than Hundreds. The Increasingly Serious Position of Xinjiang is Self-Evident.

Tibet, Which is Closely Adjacent to the Southern Route of Xinjiang Province, Has Long Been Fraught with Danger. Since the Conflict Between the Panchen Lama and the Dalai Lama, the Panchen Lama Has Been Forced to Leave Tibet. The Dalai Lama Has Then Tried to Implement His Policy of Relying on Britain. On the Surface, Tibet is Still a Territory of the Republic of China, but Actual Governing Power Cannot Reach It. In Addition, the Sichuan Warlords Only Know How to Fight Among Themselves. They Have Abandoned Xikang, Which Has Already Been Designated as a Province. No Wonder the Tibetans Disregard Us.

China is in This Situation. The Development of the Northwest is Truly Imminent. The Development of the Northwest Should Prioritize the Development of the National Economy. However, the Current Northwest Economy is Very Backward. Everything Depends on the Assistance of the Southeast. In Addition, It Has Been Closed for a Long Time. Religious Politics Have Many Contradictions, Causing the Han and Hui People to Be Unable to Cooperate and the Han and Tibetans to Be Intolerant of Each Other. In the Future, If We Want to Develop the Northwest and Actively Improve the Old Economic Structure, We Should Take the Development of Railway Transportation as the Vanguard. Then, the Cultural Movement Can Be Promoted. On the One Hand, We Must Implement Clean Politics and Resolve Religious Differences. General Personnel Issues Can Then Be Advanced Step by Step to Establish Our Country's Century-Long Plan.

Japan Conducts Sky Bombing Drill 9

Using Wireless Radio to Broadcast the Live Situation of Air Combat, the Brutal and Warlike Mentality is Fully Displayed

(Tokyo) The Kanto Air Defense Exercise is About to Begin on the 9th. The Exercise of Dropping Real Bombs from Airplanes to Attack the Ground and the Live Ammunition Firing of Anti-Aircraft Guns Was Held at Yatsu Amusement Park at 11:30 This Morning. About 300,000 People Gathered in the Tsudanuma Coast Area to Visit Japan's Sky Protection in Times of Emergency. Princes Chichibu and Kan'in Both Personally Visited. At 11:20 a.m., the First Aircraft Piloted by Captain Takeda and Lieutenant Sakurai of the Hamamatsu Air Regiment and the Second Aircraft Piloted by Lieutenant Takagi and Sergeant Sasajima Appeared in the Sky. They Dropped Four 50-Kilogram Bombs on the Buoy One Mile from the Sea. Thus, the Land and Air Sides Attacked Each Other, Presenting a Grand Spectacle. The Power of the Japanese Air Force Has Been Fully Displayed. As for the Night, Anti-Aircraft Guns Continued to Attack with Live Ammunition. The Broadcasting Bureau Also Broadcast the Situation of This Battle. The Broadcaster Matsuuchi Took the Airplane and Broadcast the Live Situation of Japan's First Air Combat. (Nichi-Rengo Telegram on the 7th)

(Changchun) This Morning, a Japanese Aircraft Returned from the Battlefield and Crashed in the Air Above Kuanchengzi Airport. The Aircraft Was Completely Burned. Sergeant Ichikawa and Three Other Mechanics Were Seriously Injured and Their Lives Were in Danger. (China-Rengo Telegram on the 7th)

American Side Expresses Opinion on British Shipbuilding Plan 10

Proceeding in Accordance with Treaty Scope, There is Absolutely No Danger of Disrupting Disarmament

(Washington) American Navy Commander Stanley Claimed Tonight That the News of the British Navy Department's Plan to Increase Shipbuilding Has Absolutely No Danger of Disrupting Disarmament. Britain Has Systematically Increased Shipbuilding in Accordance with the Strength Allowed by the Treaty. Even if the Treaty Expires, It is Legitimate to Continue Its Shipbuilding Program. His Meaning is that Creating an Unsuitable Navy Wastes Money. Therefore, to Maintain a Navy, One Must Strive for its Effectiveness. (National Telegram on the 6th)

Australia Consolidates National Defense 11

Sending Military Officers to India for Training, Constructing New Coastal Batteries

Canberra Learned Today About Australia's National Defense Plan, Intending to Send Military Officers to Practice in the Indian Army, Purchase Anti-Aircraft Guns, and Build Coastal Defense Batteries to Place Nine-Inch Two-Caliber Cannons with a Range of 31,000 Yards. (Reuters Telegram on the 7th)

Japanese Military Faction Dissatisfied with Uchida's Diplomacy 12

(Tokyo) The Japanese Military Department Has Recently Been Somewhat Estranged from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. Hardliners Within the Military Department Criticize Uchida's Diplomacy as Incompetent Diplomacy. Regarding the French Statement Occupying Jiudao, the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs Wanted to Declare the Reservation of Japan's Rights and Interests, but the Military Department Advocated from a Military Standpoint that Territorial Rights are in Japan and Contended with France. Regarding British Diplomacy, Foreign Minister Uchida Wanted to Control the Export of Japanese Goods Himself, but the Military Department Advocated Maintaining the Principle of Free Trade. The Views of Both Sides Have Not Yet Converged. In Addition, the Military Department Also Cited the Expulsion of Director Shiratori of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Military Department's Loudspeaker, as a Reason to Attack the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. (China-Rengo Telegram on the 7th)

Germany Also Holds Air Defense Exercises 13

The Military Authorities in Munich Held an Air Combat Exercise Today to Accustom Citizens to Preventing Air Raids. According to the Planned Plan, After the Alarm Sounded, All Streets Were Deserted. Ten Minutes Later, Airplanes Were Seen Soaring in the Sky, Dropping Countless Dummy Bombs. The Dummy Bombs Were Made of Sandbags with a Paper Strip Attached, Stating What Kind of Bomb the Sandbag Represented. Soon, Red Cross Ambulances Appeared on the Streets. The Workers on the Cars All Wore Gas Masks, Rescuing Imaginary Injured People Everywhere. (National Telegram on the 6th)

Puppet State's Diplomatic Policy 14

(Tokyo) The Puppet Government's Recently Decided Diplomatic Policy is as Follows: 1. "Policy Towards Japan and China": European and American Countries Organize a Strong Economic Alliance to Protect Their Own Industries. "Manchukuo" Should Form an Eastern Economic Alliance with China and Japan to Counter It. "Manchukuo" Intends to Conclude a Three-Country Customs Alliance. 2. "Policy Towards Russia": The Russia-Puppet Diplomacy is Currently Underway. If the Negotiations on the Sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway Break Down, Then it Will Establish Sovereignty Over the Chinese Eastern Railway. The Responsibility for the Deterioration of Russia-Puppet Relations Lies with the Russian Side. 3. "Policy Towards Small Countries": Special Envoys from Certain Small Countries are Currently Working Hard in Manchuria to Conduct Friendly Exchanges with the Puppet Government. "Manchukuo" Also Sends Special Envoys to Siam, Afghanistan, India, Vietnam, etc. to Enhance National Relations. 4. "Policy Towards Europe and the United States": The Ministry of Foreign Affairs Sent Various Materials to the Representatives of Various Countries at the Pacific Conference Opening in Canada in Mid-August to Promote the Current Situation of the Puppet State. (Nichi-Rengo Telegram on the 7th)

Russian Oil Arrives in Yokohama 15

After a Strict Inspection by Director Morita of the Maritime Police and Others, the 10,960 Tons of Caucasus-Produced Oil Were Prepared for Unloading. Oil Delivery Began on the Morning of the 7th. (Dentsu Telegram on the 7th)

Anti-Chinese Sentiment Spreads in Mexico 16

(New York) According to the New York Times' Mexico City Dispatch, the Anti-Chinese Movement in the State of Tamaulipas, Mexico, Has Now Spread to Tampico. (Reuters Telegram on the 7th)

Hull and Roosevelt Discuss Tariff Issues as the Focus of Discussion 17

European Tariff Barriers Hinder the Development of American Trade, and the Only Way to Promote New Markets is to Seek Help from South American Countries

Hyde Park: After Returning from the Economic Conference, U.S. Secretary of State Hull Immediately Went Here to Meet with the President. During the First Meeting, Almost Everything Discussed Related to Tariff Issues and the Possibility of Signing Reciprocal Agreements with South America. It is Said that Hull Told the President that European Trade Competition is Fierce, and New Tariff Barriers are Being Implemented for Many American Goods. Therefore, If One Wants to Revive American Foreign Trade, the Current Hope is in South America. According to Reports, Hull Held Many Private Talks with Representatives of South American Countries in London, and It is Said that He Has Already Established the Basis for Concluding New Reciprocal Agreements. Although South American Countries Signed a Reciprocal Agreement with Britain at the Beginning of the Conference, They are Facing the Same Impact of Trade Barriers in Europe as the United States. Therefore, They Also Eagerly Want to Discuss Reciprocal Measures in the Western Hemisphere. It is Said that Hull Reported to the President the New Restrictions on Trade Set Up by Countries Such as France, Poland, and Portugal, Covering Almost 300 Kinds of Goods. As a Result, the European Market for American Products is Declining Day by Day, and It is Necessary to Promote its Market in the Western Hemisphere. Therefore, the President Ordered Hull to Immediately Conduct Negotiations with South America to Sign Reciprocal Agreements. Subsequently, a Statement Was Issued from the President's Private Residence, Stating That the President Hopes That a Sincere Achievement Can Be Obtained for Reciprocal Agreements. It is Generally Believed that the Meaning of This Statement Indicates That, as a Result of Private Talks in London, Some of the Agreements Previously Proposed Can Be Signed Immediately. (National Telegram on the 6th)

American Miners' Strike Still Not Over 18

Brownsville, Pennsylvania: 70,000 Coal Miners Have Now Rejected the Ceasefire Measures Agreed Upon by Their Leaders and Mine Owners Based on President Roosevelt's Mediation and Decided to Continue the Strike. The Reason Why the Miners are Dissatisfied with This Method is That the Mine Owners Do Not Recognize the Miners' Union. (Reuters Telegram on the 7th)

Private Hoarding of Gold Must Be Handed Over by Deadline 19

(Washington) U.S. Attorney General Cummings Has Scheduled the Week Starting This Thursday as the Final Deadline for Civilians to Turn in Hoarded Gold Certificates and Gold Coins. If They Still Fail to Turn Them in by the Deadline, Their Names Will Be Published, and Lawsuits Will Be Planned. According to Cummings, There Are Still Approximately 300 Million Yuan Each of Gold Certificates and Gold Coins Hoarded by Civilians. Several of Them Have Questioned Whether the Law on Turning in Gold is Constitutional and Have Challenged the Government, Waiting Quietly for Lawsuits. Therefore, the Government Will Satisfy Their Curiosity. At the Same Time, According to Leaders of the Gold Mining Industry, the Output of Gold Mines is Decreasing Daily. In March, All Gold Mines Were Intensifying Their Work Due to the Worldwide Lack of Gold Coins. The Gold Sand Produced That Month Was Worth a Total of 5 Million Yuan. Now, Because Pure Gold Must Be Completely Purchased by the Government, the Output Has Sharply Decreased. The Total Output for the Month is Less Than 4 Million Yuan. However, Because Attorney General Cummings Announced That Unrefined Ore Can Be Legally Exported, They are Currently Planning to Centralize Ore Transportation and Export Business, Asking Shipping Companies to Estimate the Ore Transportation Costs in Order to Determine Whether They Can Make a Profit. (National Telegram on the 6th)

Agenda of the Pacific Conference 20

International Trade Issues Occupy an Important Part

Banff (Canada) The Pacific Institute Conference Will Open Here Next Week. The Members of the Program Committee Have Already Arrived Here. It is Said That the Impact of International Trade Wars, Especially on the Pacific Region, Will Be an Important Part of the Agenda, Because Far Eastern Trade is Currently the Most Important Issue That Exhausts Diplomats' Minds. In Addition, According to the Preliminary Agenda, There Are Also Issues Such as the Dumping of Japanese Electrical Appliances in the United States and the Retaliation of the American Electrical Appliance Manufacturing Industry. Also, Disputes Such as the Dispute Between Britain and Japan Over Increasing Tariffs on Japanese Textiles in British Colonies Will Also Be Discussed Unless a Large Portion of the Representatives Oppose It. Others, Such as the Competition Between Mobil Oil and Shell Oil in the Far East Market and the Status of Soviet Russia in Manchuria, Are All on the List of Discussions. Representatives of Various Countries Can Also Raise Other Issues for Discussion. They Also Have the Right to Refuse to Discuss the Issues Drawn up by the Committee. (National Telegram on the 6th)

Japanese Goods Actively Seek Outlets Overseas 21

Ministry of Commerce and Industry Formulates Plan

(Tokyo) In Order to Prepare for the Opposition of Economic Groups, the Ministry of Commerce and Industry Knows That There is a Need to Change the Traditional Liberalism Policy and Adopt a Resurgent Trade Policy. Therefore, It Urgently Seeks to Expand the Communication Network. Recently, From the Perspective of the World's Realities, Passive Coordinationism Has No Practical Results. Therefore, the Markets That Have Been Obtained in the Past Have Been Lost. The Example of South Africa and Other British Colonies is Very Obvious. The Ministry of Commerce and Industry Will Not Only Support the Market but Also Intends to Further Break Through the Economic Group to Obtain New Markets. It Has Decided to Take Next Year as the First Year to Continuously Strive to Obtain New Markets in a Comprehensive Manner. The Traditional Correspondents Only Report on Market Conditions and Do Not Achieve Practical Results. In the Future, The Correspondents Will Be Abolished in Important Places, and Large-Scale Trade Officials Will Be Established to Collect Information Necessary for Developing Markets and Actively Serve as a Medium for Trade. (Dentsu Telegram on the 7th)

India-Japan Trade Conference, Japan Again Negotiates with Britain 22

Imperialism Seizes Market Warfare, British-Japanese Friendship is on the Verge of Collapse | Commentary by Russian Newspaper |

(Tokyo) The Military Department and Textile Representatives Have Expressed Dissatisfaction with the Japan-India Trade Conference. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Unable to Help Itself, Decided to Temporarily Postpone the Departure of the Representatives. The British Government Must Vow That It Will Not Change the Results of the Negotiations, Because It Will Not Attach Full Powers of Attorney to the Indian Representatives. 2. The Japanese Representatives Are Scheduled to Take the Hakusan Maru to India on August 20 and Can Arrive in Shimla on September 20. There Are Only Two Weeks Until October 10. A New Treaty Cannot Be Completed in This Short Period of Time. 3. Before the New Treaty is Established, A Way Must Be Found to Remedy the Situation, Either by Extending the Existing Treaty or by Remedying It with a Provisional Agreement. 4. If Britain Cannot Answer Clearly, Then Japan Will Also Not Be Able to Send Representatives to Negotiate This Matter. (China-Rengo Telegram on the 7th)

(Moscow) The Izvestia Newspaper Said in an Article on the Recent Disputes Between Britain and Japan That From the Beginning of This Century Until the Washington Conference in 1921, the Relationship Between Britain and Japan Was Actually a Vivid Picture Showing the Friendship Between Two Aggressive Imperialist Powers. This Friendship Still Makes Britain Shield Japan's Conquest of Manchuria. The Newspaper Continued That Recently, However, British-Japanese Relations Have Become Tense Due to the Fierce Competition for Markets. The Newspaper Quoted Figures to Show How Japan is Crowding Britain Out of the Colonial Market and How Japanese Goods are Competing with British Goods (Even in England Itself) and Winning. It Said That the Conflict Between Britain and Japan in the Economic Field is Obviously Becoming More and More Fierce. All Efforts at Compromise Have Obviously Been Declared a Failure. The Newspaper Concluded, "We Cannot Doubt That British and Japanese Imperialism Still Maintain Their Consistency in Many Important Places. However, Their Economic Competition Has Placed Their Traditional Friendship at the Top of Extreme Difficulty." (TASS Telegram on the 6th)

Fighting in the Minjiang River Intensifies 24

Mei, Peng, Xin and Other County Towns are Bombed, Liu Xiang Proposes Three Methods to Liu Wenhui

(Nanjing) A Military Agency Received a Telegram from Chengdu on the 6th, Saying That the Fighting Along the Minjiang River Has Gradually Intensified Since the 1st. In Recent Days, County Towns such as Mei, Peng, and Xin, as Well as Houses on Both Sides of the River, Have Been Greatly Damaged by Aircraft Bombs. At Dawn on the 3rd, There Was Fierce Fighting at Yuedianzi, Shuanghechang, Tangheba, Yanguan Between Xin and Zizhong and Jiangjiadu and Wangdu Between Peng and Mei. The Attack on Chenjiadu, Chuanxindian, and Shujiadu Along the Jinma River Was Also Very Fierce. The Artillery War in the Jiading Area Has Not Yet Stopped. (Special Dispatch on the 7th)

(Nanjing) Liu Xiang Telegraphed His Representative in Beijing on the 7th, Saying That Liu Wenhui's Troops Are Still Gathered on the Right Bank of the Minjiang River, Holding Each Other Across the River. Although His Generals Have Telegraphed Separately, Expressing Their Willingness to Accept the Scope, They Have Not Yet Proposed Practical Methods That Can Be Solved Due to Environmental Constraints. In This Confrontational Situation, If We Hastily Transfer Troops to Suppress the Bandits, I am Afraid That the Remnants of the Liu-Deng Dispute Will Reignite. Therefore, Referring to the Intentions of the Generals in the Previous and Subsequent Telegrams, I Propose Three Methods: 1. Zi Gan Leads a Part of the Troops to Specialize in Defending Xikang and Must Move Quickly. 2. The Remaining Troops Should Be Commanded by Xiang to Suppress the Bandits, So That They Can Immediately Express Their Telegrams, or Change Their Flags and Set Off One After Another. 3. In Order to Promote the Foregoing Methods, Our Army Must First Cross the River with a Part of the Troops to Facilitate Supervision and Implement the Above Articles. I Have Telegraphed These to Zi Gan and His Generals. If They Can Be Solved in This Way, They Can Eliminate Internal Strife and Join Forces to Suppress the Red Bandits. Relying on the Central Government's Virtue, They May Be Able to Comply as Scheduled. (Special Dispatch on the 7th)

Issuing 65 Million Yuan in Public Bonds

(Nanjing) The Jiaoji Railway Decided on a Road Redemption Plan and Reported It to the Ministry of Railways. It is Proposed That Starting from the 23rd Year, the Monthly Surplus of About 2 Million Yuan Will Be Used to Fund the Road Redemption. It is Also Proposed to Issue 65 Million Yuan in Public Bonds with the Road Assets as Collateral. 40 Million Will Be Used to Redeem the Road, and 25 Million Will Be Used to Build the Zhangde Branch Line. It is Expected That the Public Bonds Can Be Repaid After 25 Years. It is Said That the Ministry of Railways Plans to Put It on File. (Central News Agency Telegram on the 7th)

From the World Economic Conference to China's Way Out 27

Ju Zheng's Report at the National Government Memorial Week (Nanjing) The National Government's Memorial Week was held on the 7th. Chen Shaokuan, et al., attended. Chairman Lin Sen, Ju Zheng gave a report titled "From the Failure of the World Economic Conference to China's Way Out," which stated in brief: There were many reasons for the failure of this World Economic Conference. Due to the conflicting interests and stances of various countries, the Economic Conference ended in a disastrous failure. In the future, the tariff exchange dumping wars of various countries will inevitably be fiercer than before. All countries feel overproduction, and it is imperative to strive for exports. The only way is to intensify the control of the economy and strengthen military power. The former seeks temporary stability at home, and the latter is the backing for winning the market. In fact, what is revealed to us is not the lack of production, but the uneven distribution. Under this particularly difficult environment in our country, if we adopt free capitalism, it will only seek the interests of a few people. The Prime Minister has elaborated on this. If we adopt socialist economic policies, although Soviet Russia has achieved good results with this, China is in the international market dominated by international capitalism, it is inevitable that it will be difficult to succeed. The attempt to save the country must not be pinned on dreams. Only developing national capitalism is the only important plan, and it must be controlled by the state. The methods are: (1) Investigate what is lacking in the production index; (2) Investigate cash to clarify the national financial resources; (3) Pay attention to the development of national capital.

Under the condition that sovereignty and interests are not hindered, use foreign forces to assist in production. Recently, there have been two things that have caused misunderstandings among the people, namely borrowing money from the United States and cooperating with the League of Nations. The government has clearly declared the purpose of the former. Although there is obstruction from Japan in the latter, I hope that you will not believe its rumors, which will lead to speculation about handing over production undertakings to international co-management. In short, when the struggle between the great powers is becoming more acute and the Second World War is more imminent, we should develop national capital under state control in order to survive. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 7th)

Song Concluded Loan Negotiations for National Steel Plant in Germany 28

Formal Contract to be Signed After Returning Home (Nanjing) Huang Jinxuan, the director of the Mining Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, said that the loan issue for the Central Iron and Steel Plant has been negotiated with the German Xiwang Company. He also telegraphed Minister Song to solicit opinions. Song recently replied by telegram, saying that he had completed negotiations with the company in Germany, and that a formal loan contract would be signed after his return home, etc. Everything is now ready, and the factory site has also been decided at Ma'anshan, and will not be changed. Construction can begin after the contract is signed. The rumor that it has stalled is completely untrue. (Special dispatch on the 7th)

Tang Shaoyi Discusses the Importance of the Nine Small Islands 29

Navy Will Not Send Ships to Investigate for the Time Being (Hong Kong) Tang Shaoyi talked about the occurrence of the Nine Islands case, and the Guangdong authorities paid great attention to it and held meetings to discuss it for several days. The island is the throat of Qiongzhou Island. If it is not recovered, it will have a great impact on our country's fishery and will lose national sovereignty. The central and southwest authorities should find ways to recover the island no matter what. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 7th)

(Nanjing) Chen Shaokuan told reporters on the 7th that the Navy is investigating the French occupation of the Nine Small Islands and that there is no need to send ships there for the time being. If necessary, the Navy can send ships to conduct on-site investigations at any time. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 7th)

(Nanjing) The Navy is studying the longitude and latitude of the Xisha Nine Small Islands being occupied, as well as previous negotiation files. A concrete report will be available soon. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has telegraphed our country's consul in the Philippines to investigate nearby. Therefore, the Navy will not send ships for the time being. As for the case of the French Consulate in Tianjin occupying our naval hospital, Foreign Minister Wei Liding came to Nanjing this time, and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs once discussed it with him, requesting the French Consul in Tianjin to refrain from excessive actions, which would damage the friendship between the two countries. (Special dispatch on the 7th)

Credentials Issued to Economic Conference Delegation 30

Yan Huiqing Will Return Home for a Visit (Nanjing) The credentials of the delegation to the London Economic Conference have been approved by the National Government and ordered the Executive Yuan to forward them to the recipient. (Special dispatch on the 7th)

Yan Huiqing in Leningrad told reporters that the London Conference was fruitless, but the arrival of Finance Minister Song gave Europeans and Americans a good impression. China signed a silver price agreement, which can stabilize the silver price and increase purchasing power. Yan will stay here for about four days and then return to Moscow. He also plans to go to southern Russia for inspection. Because he has been away from the country for a long time, he decided to return home for a visit. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 6th)

Establishment of the Sino-Dutch Geng Fund Board of Directors 31

First Meeting Held Yesterday (Nanjing) The Sino-Dutch Geng Fund Board of Directors held its inaugural meeting at the Nanjing Municipal Government on the 7th. Shi Ying, the chairman of the board, Sun Shifu of the Taihu Lake Conservancy Commission, and Grohman, the Dutch Consul in Shanghai, attended. After Shi reported on the distribution of the returned portion of the Sino-Dutch Geng Fund, the first meeting was held immediately. Resolutions: (1) The Dutch Geng Fund will be allocated for the preliminary engineering plan of Nanjing City's water conservancy. After the Dutch engineer arrives in Nanjing, it will be implemented after careful consideration. (2) The Dutch government will be requested by letter from the Dutch Consul to dispatch an engineer immediately to Nanjing before September 1 to facilitate the progress of Nanjing City's water conservancy project. (3) A letter to the Dutch government to investigate Chinese leprosy patients and send them back to China for treatment. (4) It is stipulated that the board of directors will hold a meeting once in January and June each year. French Aviators Make Non-Stop Long-Distance Flights 68

Continuing East After Crossing the Atlantic, There is Hope to Break the World Record

National News Agency Strasbourg telegram on the 7th: After French aviators Rossi and Codou set off from New York on the morning of the 5th, although they carried a lot of oil, they made rapid progress. They did not encounter any other obstacles except for light wind and rain along the way. At 6 pm on the 6th, they had flown over Cherbourg, France, and were heading towards the Le Bourget airport outside Paris. At 8:20, they passed Paris and proceeded towards Munich, Germany. They passed Munich at midnight. According to the latest radio from the plane, they had arrived twenty miles south of Vienna at 1:50 am this morning and were advancing towards Belgrade. However, after the plane passed Munich, the Paris radio station received their radio, saying that there was an obstruction in the oil pipeline and they wanted a guide to guide them to the Alps. It is estimated that the oil pipeline has been repaired in the sky, so they went straight to Belgrade.

Havas Paris telegram on the 6th: Regarding the long-distance flight of Rossi and Codou, the newspapers here pointed out that the previous world record for the longest straight-line flight was 8,544 kilometers. According to the regulations of the International Aeronautical Federation, Rossi and Codou must fly more than 100 kilometers before they can be recognized as breaking the previous record. When the two flew over the Le Bourget airport, they had flown 5,780 kilometers. The remaining gasoline can still be used for three hours of flight. At a speed of 160 kilometers per hour, they can still fly 4,800 kilometers, totaling more than 10,000 kilometers, which is more than enough to break the world record.

Reuters Vienna telegram on the 7th: French aviators Rossi and Codou set off from New York on Saturday morning, hoping to break the current British record of 5,340 miles for non-stop long-distance flight. They have now flown over Romania and are heading towards Aleppo in Asian Turkey. Their plane's fuel is running out. The two plan to reach Aleppo before the fuel supply runs out. If they fail to reach the city, the attempt to break the record will fail. They sent out a radio message saying that the oil consumption was beyond normal, probably due to an oil wave leak. Vienna also received their latest report, stating that they had flown to Rhodes in the Aegean Sea, which is not far from the southern coast of Asia Minor. Reuters Paris telegram on the 7th: According to non-official news from Aleppo, the two French aviators flew over the city of Aleppo at 1:30 pm today. If so, the British record of 5,340 miles for non-stop long-distance flight has been broken by the French aviators.

Hitler's Speech on Foreign and Domestic Affairs 69

Berlin, August 6th (By Wireless from Platterschloss-Gartens): Today, German leader Adolf Hitler delivered a lengthy speech, lasting three hours, to key party members attending a meeting of local leaders. He discussed the economic, foreign, political, and domestic situations. He stated, "The restoration of domestic order is intimately related to Germany's position in the world. The power to govern the nation must be consolidated into a solid system, free from all external interference. The power of the Nazi movement must not be bound by any individual but must be built on a foundation that guarantees its permanent existence. Therefore, he proposes organizing a Senate comprised of senior and most trusted party members, from which will emanate the sacred authority of the leader." Hitler also said, "To return to our roots, the Nazi Party headquarters will henceforth be permanently located in Munich, and the annual Nazi Party Day commemoration will always be held in Nuremberg." He continued, "Regarding the economic problems the nation is currently facing, I will briefly describe our strategy for a frontal assault on the economic adversity, which will be carried out in three steps. The first step has already seen two million unemployed find work. The second step is scheduled to begin in September, with financial preparations already in place. This move aims to maintain the achievements of this summer. The third step will be implemented next spring, at which time unemployment will be further reduced." Hitler concluded by saying, "Looking to the future, it fills me with endless hope."

Italian Ship Salvages Sunken Gold 70

Worth £36,000 – Reuters, London, August 7: The Italian salvage ship "Artiglio" arrived in Plymouth today carrying gold and silver worth £36,000. This treasure was salvaged from the British company mail ship "Egypt," which sank in the English Channel in 1922. It is reported that the sunken ship was carrying gold and silver worth over a million pounds, including 1,089 gold bars in 122 boxes, weighing over four and a half tons, and 37 boxes of gold coins, valued at £164,949. In addition, there were 43 tons of silver, totaling 1,299 bars, each weighing approximately 60-70 pounds. The recovery of this gold and silver is the result of over three years of effort by the Italian salvage ship.

The Hua Dong Republic's Plan to Overthrow the Puppet State 71

(Aiming to Eliminate Japanese Influence in the Northeast Within Six Years)

Harbin Special Dispatch: The five districts designated by the Hua Dong Republic are: (1) Central District, (2) Eastern Jilin District, (3) Eastern Heilongjiang District, (4) Eastern Liaoning District, and (5) Far East District. These five districts are not the definitively established territories of the Republic, but rather temporary military divisions to facilitate the separate promotion of the Republic's establishment. Not only the Chinese people, but all oppressed nationalities of the Far East are participating. The main purpose is to overthrow the puppet organizations fostered by the Japanese. The process is divided into two phases, each lasting three years. The first phase will focus on completing the construction of the Northeastern mountainous regions, overthrowing the puppet state's organization and construction, and simultaneously eliminating all Japanese military and political influence in the Northeast. It also includes organizing a genuinely popular nation and liberating all oppressed and weak nationalities. From July 1, 1936, the second phase will commence, taking advantage of the outbreak of the Second World War to gain belligerent status. Given that the war should not last more than three years, the Republic's territory will be twice the size of present-day Germany. With maximum effort, the Korean people can definitely achieve their liberation goals, after which they can engage in construction. According to those familiar with Guo Daofu, Guo now bears heavy political responsibilities for the Hua Dong Republic. Guo is a Dahuur Mongol and graduated from the First Middle School of Heilongjiang Province. He then went to the Russian Law and Politics School in Beijing. After graduating, he transferred to Peking University. Before graduating, he went to the Northeast to engage in revolutionary work. Later, he went to Russia for study and gained valuable insights. Upon returning to Outer Mongolia, he advocated national self-determination and sought to liberate the Mongolian people, organizing the Outer Mongolian Republic, and serving as Minister of the Interior. In 1928, he attempted independence in Hulunbuir and once came to Beijing, but the central government, due to various reasons, did not receive him. He then returned to Liaoning to found the Mongolian Banner Normal School, which achieved great success. Guo is now only forty years old, talented and knowledgeable, fluent in Chinese, Mongolian, English, Russian, and Japanese, and is known as the "Sage of Mongolia." (Northeast News Agency)

Inspection Report on Jiangxi, Anhui, Hunan, and Hubei by Our Special Correspondent, Ren An 72

The Seemingly Strong But Inwardly Weak Commerce of Zhangshu

Zhangshu Special Dispatch: Zhangshu Town belongs to Qingjiang County. Its convenient transportation and developed commerce make it not only the economic center of Qingjiang (some have proposed moving the county seat here) but also a strategically important location controlling the two major river basins of the Gan River and Yuan River. The Gan-Yue highway line, running straight north-south, has a station here, further increasing its transportation convenience. Therefore, since the suppression of bandits began, elite troops have been stationed here regularly. In 1930, Zhu De and Mao Zedong led their main force to attack once, extorting 60,000 yuan from the Chamber of Commerce, but they were soon repelled by the National Army. Immediately, wooden walls, earthen walls, and outer moats were added to the defensive works. Recently, construction of bunkers and outer moats has begun, and barbed wire has been added (military obstacles). From now on, the defense of Zhangshu Town will be as solid as a rock.

The shops and stores in Zhangshu City are mostly three- or four-story cement buildings with glass windows and wax figure decorations, quite impressive. Walking from Zhongshan Gate straight to the large wharf on the Gan River, looking left and right, one might almost think one is on Dazhong Road in Jiujiang or Fourth Avenue in Shanghai. Its prosperity can be imagined. However, revealing the inner workings of its commerce, such as the sharp annual decline in trade volume and the invisible bankruptcies of stores, causes one to worry deeply about the future of its commerce. The rice-producing areas of Jiangxi province are mostly in the Gan and Yuan River basins, but all the rice is gathered here and then distributed to Jiujiang, Hankou, and other places, amounting to about 200,000 dan per year. Jiangxi is a major producer of medicinal herbs, and all herbs entering and leaving the province must also be collected here. The medicinal herb business has an annual trade value of over two million yuan. Other goods, such as timber, melon seeds, soybeans, wheat, and imported foreign goods, also each have an annual turnover of about one million yuan. Now, because various counties have been banditized, taxes and levies are frequent, and the people suffer from soldiers and bandits. The people's purchasing power has gradually declined, making it difficult for goods to come in and difficult for goods to go out. The annual volume of trade is less than one-third of what it used to be, and timber merchants have suffered particularly heavy losses. The number of unemployed people in the county has reached ten thousand. The shops in Zhangshu City may appear prosperous on the outside, but this is not true prosperity in business. Rather, it is competition in promotion. The expenses exceed the income in eight or nine out of ten cases. High-interest loans are even more prevalent than in the countryside. Among those whose businesses are losing money, debts are piling up, and even if they want to formally declare bankruptcy, they cannot. Last year, there were still fifteen money shops, some with capital of up to 200,000 yuan, but after only one year, they have all collapsed, leaving only eight. There are also many other businesses that cannot open and cannot close.

The county levies as many as twenty-one different taxes and levies, not counting the regular land tax. These include doorplate tax, porter tax, airplane surveying tax, telephone tax, Jishui bridge tax, defense tax, "iron shoulder" team tax, highway tax, soldier allowance tax, grain storage tax, chamber of commerce tax, aviation tax, bunker tax, baojia tax, wooden wall tax, volunteer team tax, superstition tax (only levied on Taoist priests, etc.), stamp tax (each business must affix a certain amount each month), public security fee (in Zhangshu Town, it is paid from prostitution tax), opium suppression tax (only levied on those with opium addiction who have obtained an opium suppression license from the Special Tax Bureau), and dike construction tax. The amount of money to be paid for each of the above taxes and levies, as well as whether to pay all of them or only some of them, varies depending on the time and place.

This is not only the case in one county. All counties near bandit areas are the same. As for what Zhangshu Town pays, according to the chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, since 1926, it has been up to 120,000-130,000 yuan at most each year, and at least 20,000-30,000 yuan. There are also requisitions of goods (such as hay, sacks, hoes, boats, etc.), which are not included.

In 1930, the Red Bandits attacked Zhangshu. Mao Zedong, resembling a cook, gave a speech on the stage of the Tianhou Palace, bewitching the people. Later, the Chamber of Commerce, using the name of the local community, pawned goldware at the Huili and Binxing public pawnshops (the pawned items) and raised 60,000 yuan in silver dollars at a price of fifty taels, which was given to the Red Army. Although a catastrophe of burning, killing, and destruction was avoided at that time, the suffering of the townspeople when they raised the original items at a gold price of sixty or seventy taels afterward cannot be fully described in a few words.

The prostitution tax is about 18-19 yuan per prostitute per month. During peak months, a total of 800-900 yuan is collected, while during slow months, only half that amount is collected. Opium smoking licenses are handled by the Jiangxi Office of the Hubei Special Tax Bureau. Each license costs five yuan and is limited to one person, with the fee doubling each subsequent half-year period. Zhangshu Town has two opium dens. It is said that each den pays a license fee of 400 yuan, as well as various fees for stamps, safekeeping, transportation, and anti-smuggling.

The exact amount of each of these fees is unknown. Zhangshu Town has a population of over 20,000, with smokers accounting for about 5% of the population. Some say that if only the male population is counted, it is probably more than that. If this trend continues, it is tantamount to suicide. Discussing this, knowledgeable people cannot help but feel chilled. (August 1st)

Southern Route Army to Besiege Junmenling 73

(Bandits Stationed at Junmenling Led by Ye Jianying)

(The Southern Route Army Advances with Elite Troops)

Shantou Telegram: Junmenling in Jiangxi Province, located in Huichang County, is an important market town for land trade between the three provinces of Fujian, Guangdong, and Jiangxi, and has long been occupied by the Communist Party as a base for harassing the borders of Fujian and Guangdong. When the Second Column of the Southern Route Army initially attacked Xunwu a few days ago, the Communist bandit Ye Jianying immediately stationed troops on the ridge to support the bandits of Changting and Xunwu. Ye is a native of Meixian, Guangdong, and is a key figure in the bandit group. He is currently the Commander-in-Chief and Principal of the Pseudo-Military Political Protection Training Corps and Military Academy. Recently, the main forces of Zhu De and Mao Zedong's Pseudo-135th Army Corps gathered in the mountains on the Fujian-Jiangxi border, planning to resist the Southern Route Bandit Suppression Army. Therefore, Ye Jianying was assigned to station at Junmenling to provide support. However, the opponents of the Southern Route Army who fought against Ye were also natives of Meixian, namely Huang Renhuan, the commander of the First Independent Division, Huang Yanzhen, the commander of the Seventh Division, and Huang Zhiwen, the commander of the Eighth Division. They are all quite familiar with the terrain of the mountains on the border of Fujian, Guangdong, and Jiangxi. Because Ye's tactics are fierce and he often uses desperate measures and takes risks, the Southern Route Army is advancing step by step. Huang Zhiwen's division of Xunwu and Jitan has been fighting fiercely with the main force of Ye's Pseudo-12th Division since July 15th. Huang Yanzhen came to the rescue via Xiangshan, and Huang Renhuan came to the rescue via Luotang, engaging in extremely fierce battles. Ye's bandits finally retreated to Huichang on the 18th due to exhaustion of ammunition and food. Another unit retreated north from Chengjiangxu, passing through Xitou, Wuping, and was intercepted by Ye Weihou's brigade of Huang Renhuan's unit, killing forty or fifty male and female bandits, capturing three male bandits and seven female bandits, and seizing twelve rifles. Currently, the territory of Xunwu County has been gradually cleared, but Ye's bandits are still gathered on the line of Junmenling and Huichang, with the determination to defend to the death. On the 28th, the entire unit of Huang Yanzhen also entered the Wanyu and Jitan area from Pingyuan. The defense of Pingyuan was taken over by Deng Hui's unit of the Training Corps. The armies are converging on Junmenling and advancing cautiously. The greatest goal is to support the 19th Route Army in besieging Changting. If Junmenling is taken back by the Southern Route Army, the bandits of Changting will be threatened. If Changting falls, the Fujian-Guangdong armies can be connected in a straight line, and the puppet capital of Ruijin can be attacked. The Fifth Squadron of the Air Force stationed in Meixian has flown to Jiaoling, and Meixian is also preparing to build a large barracks that can accommodate two regiments. It is expected that there will be a fierce battle on Junmenling. (August 2nd)

Xiaoshan Jail's Evil Prisoner Violently Assaults Guard 74

Since Warden Su took office at the county jail, he has eliminated abuses such as corrupt practices and gangsterism. The dark hell is gradually seeing the light of day. Last month, fifty sentenced prisoners were sent from Suzhou, most of whom were from Anhui and had been bandits in the Taihu area. They were extremely fierce, and weak prisoners were often bullied and oppressed in every way. Recently, three of the most vicious criminals, Kong Xiaoheshang, Gu Mingxin, and Zhao Heiyu, dared to meet with the jail supervisors and request to be appointed as head prisoners so that they could openly extort new prisoners. Supervisor Su informed them that head prisoners had long been abolished here and rejected their request. The criminals then secretly incited the prisoners and, taking advantage of the opportunity to open the cells yesterday, suddenly created a disturbance and assaulted the guard Jiang Faming, threatening to gouge out his eyes. The situation was tense. Guard Jiang shouted for help. Supervisor Su reported to the county government and the procuratorate. Subsequently, the county government dispatched twenty police officers, and the court also sent Prosecutor Zhu to provide guidance. With the suppression of the police, Guard Jiang's danger was resolved. It is understood that Supervisor Su has submitted a document to the county government for review.

Wuxi Teenage Traveler Commits Suicide by Taking Poison 75

On the afternoon of the 6th, a young traveler arrived at the New World Hotel on Tongyun Road, claiming to be Lian Dequan, a native of Zhenru, 19 years old, and a timber merchant. He opened room number 63. Unexpectedly, after entering the room, Lian immediately closed the door and swallowed four opium pills. By about 11 o'clock, the poison had taken effect. The tea attendant noticed and reported to the bookkeeper, who carried him to Tongren Hospital for treatment. However, because he had been poisoned deeply, he died on the way. His body was then carried to the Hotel Association on Dongxin Road, and the relevant Public Security Second Branch was notified to send police to the hotel to inspect his belongings. There was a suicide note addressed to Hua Mingfu of Hengfengxiang Timber Company outside Qimen, Suzhou, signed by Lian Jizhi. The letter stated the reason for the suicide, saying that he was under financial pressure and could not have freedom in marriage. The hotel telegraphed Suzhou and reported it to the court, which went to inspect the body on the morning of yesterday.

Hangzhou Wangjiangmen Outside Robbery Case Criminals Arrested 76

The case of Zhu Youfu's home at No. 8 Datong Bridge outside Wangjiangmen in Hangzhou being robbed of more than 200 silver dollars on the evening of the 30th of last month has been reported in this newspaper. After the case occurred, Director He ordered the detectives to solve the case within five days. Detective Zhou Kang, accompanied by Wang Fugen, a member of the Wangjiangmen Outer Security Corps, arrested the criminal Wang Dehui in the case at Erliangting at 1:20 pm the day before yesterday. Under interrogation by Captain Tang Shihhu, Wang confessed directly to carrying a gun to commit the robbery, but said that he only received 23 yuan of the loot. Eighty-five yuan of counterfeit banknotes from the Bank of Communications, ten yuan of counterfeit banknotes from the Central Bank, and fourteen two-jiao counterfeit banknotes were found on him. He also confessed that the wooden-cased gun was hidden at Li Guocai's place, so Li was also arrested. Wang Dehui had stayed in room number 2 of the Yongan Hotel in Xinshi Market for a few days after the robbery. Therefore, Captain Tang, for the sake of caution, immediately summoned the victim Zhu Youfu and the tea attendant Lu Jintang of the Yongan Hotel to the case to testify. They confirmed that the criminal had first entered with a gun and restrained the old woman before committing the robbery. Tea attendant Lu Jintang also testified that the criminal Wang Dehui had stayed at the hotel for a few days. After further questioning by Captain Zhu, it was confirmed to be accurate. Yesterday (the 7th) morning, he was sent to the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau for verification.

Nantong Professor Accuses Japanese Wife of Murder Attempt 77

Huang Yulun, a medical professor at Nantong University, married a Japanese woman named Otsuka Kaneko when he studied in Japan in previous years. They have been married for nine years and have three children. Huang teaches in Nantong, and his wife and children live with him in the Nantong Hospital apartment affiliated with the medical school. Recently, the relationship between the couple suddenly deteriorated. Otsuka Kaneko chased Huang Yulun with a kitchen knife, saying that she would kill Huang and then commit suicide. Huang was greatly frightened and has taken his three children to take refuge in the Nantong Club Hotel. He has also hired a lawyer to sue his wife for attempted murder. The procuratorate has approved the case and scheduled a hearing for investigation.

Westener Drowns Swimming in Sea in Pinghu 78

Since the Huangshan area of Zhapu was developed as a summer resort, there has been a constant stream of cars from Shanghai and Hangzhou. Each day more and more Chinese and foreigners enjoy swimming in the sea there for recreation. Yesterday, a Westerner went into the sea to bathe, not understanding the nature of the tides. He was tossed about by the waves. Onlookers were unable to help. In an instant, he was carried away by the tide. Those who saw it were all horrified. This is written as a warning to those who play in the sea in the future.

Fire Destroys Xiaoshan Fishing Family's Home, Killing Two Children 79

On the night of the 5th, a fire broke out at the home of fisherman Dong Yongnian on the bank of the West Xiaojiang River due to careless use of mosquito coils. Coupled with the hot weather, rescue was difficult. Two houses and six flat houses were completely destroyed in a short time. Most tragically, two children, aged eight and five, were unable to escape and died in the fire.

Song Zheyuan Sends Telegram to Obey Orders and Take Charge of the Chahar Situation 81

Huang Fu's Arrival in Shanghai Is to Handle Personal Affairs

Since the arrival of Song Zheyuan, the chairman of the Chahar Province government, in Shacheng, the negotiations have been quite satisfactory. Feng Yuxiang immediately issued a telegram, returning military and political power to the central government. The Chahar situation, which seemed to be on the verge of crisis, has thus come to an end. As for the aftermath, Chairman Song is solely responsible for handling it. Rumors that the focus of the Chahar situation has shifted to Shanghai and that Huang Fu will come to Shanghai to meet with Li Liejun to discuss concrete solutions to the Chahar situation are not accurate. The details are as follows:

Song Zheyuan Shanghai Municipal Government received a telegram yesterday from Song Zheyuan, Chairman of Chahar Province, stating: (Handling the aftermath) (Telegram truncated, briefly stating an invitation for inspection). After arriving in Chahar, General Feng stated in a telegram that Chahar Province had someone in charge and that all military and civilian affairs had been returned to the central government and that he would not interfere. Zheyuan will immediately obey orders and be responsible for handling everything. This telegram is respectfully submitted and awaits instructions. Song Zheyuan bows, Seal.

Huang Yingbai's Mission to Shanghai

It has been widely rumored in Shanghai that Huang Yingbai, Chairman of the Political Reorganization Committee of the Executive Yuan stationed in Beiping, will come to Shanghai to meet with Central Committee member Li Liejun to discuss concrete solutions. However, according to those close to Huang who have just arrived in Shanghai from Beiping, Mr. Huang does indeed intend to come to Shanghai, but it is to handle personal affairs and not to meet with Mr. Li to discuss solutions to the Chahar situation. This is because concrete solutions to the Chahar situation were agreed upon on the spot by Song Zheyuan in Shacheng, meeting with Feng Yuxiang's representatives, Sun Liangcheng and Tong Linge. There is no need for Huang to come to Shanghai to meet with Li.

Chairman Chiang's Reply Telegram Arrives in Shanghai 82

After Li Xiehe forwarded Feng's telegram to Wang and Chiang, he sent another telegram the next day inquiring about the concrete measures under the four principles. Yesterday, he received a reply telegram from Chiang, briefly stating that the concrete measures for the Chahar situation are under discussion and will be telegraphed again upon a decision. The most important measure for the aftermath is the placement of the more than 100,000 troops in Chahar Province who resisted Japan.

Li Liejun Issues a Statement 83

Since Li Xiehe telegraphed the central government to report Feng Huanzhang's telegram, Chairman Lin, Premier Wang, Director Yu, and Chairman Chiang have successively sent telegrams to Shanghai praising the matter and hoping that Li will continue his efforts. The Chahar situation is now showing signs of harmony. Correspondents from various news agencies visited Mr. Li at his private residence yesterday morning to inquire about everything. He issued the following statement: Since the Japanese invaders have driven into our country, who in the country is not indignant? Huanzhang's uprising in Zhangjiakou after the government reluctantly signed the agreement was not only courageous but also wise. Within a few dozen days, people flocked to him, and the disorderly masses became a disciplined army. Enemy generals surrendered, and the people loved him. Those with ambition thought of returning to him. Therefore, he was able to recover four counties with a proclamation and capture Duolun in one battle. This is rare in modern history. The whole country admires him. Therefore, it is right. The government is responsible for defending the land and did not willingly lose it. It was because it wanted to plan before acting that it could not support Huanzhang's actions. Such is the state of the nation. It is also unfortunate. The disaster of civil war is even worse. I admire Huanzhang's courageous action and unwillingness to compromise in the face of difficulty, and I also appreciate the government's patience and forbearance. Therefore, I gave the government unwelcome advice and waited for the opportunity to act for Huanzhang. Now they have been adopted. This is not only my personal fortune. Now that Huanzhang has accepted the proposals of Wang and Chiang, he has also returned political power to Song. Huanzhang has done everything that he should have done. However, Huanzhang cannot ignore the more than 100,000 patriotic soldiers who resisted Japan. How will they be treated well and kept in reserve for the future to restore the country and avenge the shame of the nation? Therefore, I emphasized this point in my previous telegram to the government and Chairman Chiang. I also said that the government should regard Huanzhang as the Great Wall and give him great power to take on important responsibilities. Soon, I received a reply telegram from Mr. Chiang agreeing with my view and forwarding it to the central government. This matter is still under discussion. Whether it is handled in the front or negotiated separately, the big things have been turned into small things, and the small things have been turned into nothing. Our hope is not only to seek peace in the Chahar situation but also to properly plan for the stability of the whole country. Therefore, the government's future measures may have to adhere more to the scope of democratic politics.

Langguan's Public Visit to Ma, Returning to Shanghai 87

Ma Gushan stayed at Moganshan for quite some time, and the commemorative album of the anti-Japanese war record will soon be published. Gao Hang Agricultural Association Prevents and Controls Locust Nymphs 88

The Great Rain May Eradicate Them Without a Trace Since the Beginning of Summer, the Weather in This City Has Been Very Dry, and Rice Seedlings Have Been Difficult to Grow. Farmers Are Generally Concerned About a Poor Harvest. As a Result of the Prolonged Drought, Locust Plagues Have Occurred. Locust Nymphs Have Already Been Discovered in the Farmland of Various Districts in Pudong. After Receiving a Report from the Gao Hang District Agricultural Association Yesterday, the Municipal Agricultural Association Immediately Issued an Order to All District Agricultural Associations to Pay Attention to Prevention and Control, and Requested the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau to Prepare to Purchase Them at a Price to Eliminate the Locust Plague. Fortunately, There Was Heavy Rain Yesterday, Which May Eradicate Them Without a Trace, and the Gao Hang District Agricultural Association Has Issued a Notice to Farmers to Prevent and Control Locust Plagues and Advise Them to Prepare.

Yu Shun Steamer That Was Robbed Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday Morning 89

Sixteen Crew Members and Others Are Suspected of Colluding with Bandits and Were Arrested in Shantou; Three Kidnapped People Are Missing; Total Loss Is Approximately Over Ten Thousand Yuan. The China Merchants Bureau's Yu Shun Steamer Was Robbed Last Month in Southern Shantou by Bandits Disguised as Passengers and Fled to Haifeng. Before Leaving, They Also Kidnapped Three Staff Members and Passengers. It Was Later Discovered That the Steamer's Crew Was Suspected of Colluding With Bandits. When Returning to Shantou, Military Police Arrested Sixteen Crew Members and Others. The Steamer Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday Morning and Docked at Jinliyuan Wharf. The Detailed Circumstances Are Recorded Below:

(Warning Before Departure and Robbery Process) The Yu Shun Steamer Sailed From Guangzhou Last Month. An Alert Had Been Received in Advance Stating That the Crew Was Colluding With Bandits and Attempting to Rob the Ship. Military Police Conducted an Inspection, But Found Nothing Suspicious. Therefore, It Departed On Time. On the Morning of the 31st of Last Month, It Arrived in Shantou Via Hong Kong and Unloaded Goods as Usual. At 6 PM That Evening, It Departed From Shantou to Xiamen. Unexpectedly, Before It Had Sailed Thirty Miles South of Shantou, Pirates Who Had Been Lying in Ambush in the Hold Immediately Launched an Attack. Because No Shots Were Fired and No Special Signals Were Made, the Crew Was Caught Off Guard and the Bandits Broke Into the Bridge. Another Group of Pirates Invaded the Engine Room and the Radio Room, Destroying the Electrical Machinery With Axes. Then They Drove the Crew and Passengers Into the Stern Hold and Imprisoned Them. They Forced the Engine Room Personnel to Sail to Haifeng. After Three Robberies Overnight, They Arrived in Haifeng at Noon the Next Day. The Pirates Seized a Fisherman's Sailboat, and Transferred the Kidnapped Victims and Stolen Goods to the Sailboat, And Escaped to Honghai Bay. After the Yu Shun Steamer Saw the Pirates Escape, It Turned Back to Shantou and Arrived at 7 AM on the Second. At That Time, Because the Crew Was Suspected of Colluding With Bandits, It Was Reported to the Shantou Military Police, Who Arrested and Interrogated Them. The Arrested Crew Members Were Li Shaoting, Li Guocheng, Chen Shengguan, Xu Yaoke, Xie Aqi, Li Chengren, Lu Ajin, Qian Ashun, Zhou Jinzhang, Jiang Baosheng, Hu Ahong, All Ningbo People; Accountant Fang Jinhuai; Passenger Solicitor Cai Huatang; and Three Passengers. After Clearing the Ship, The Yu Shun Steamer Sailed to Xiamen On the 4th and Departed From Xiamen to Shanghai On the 5th, Arriving in Shanghai at 7:30 AM Yesterday. It Docked at Jinliyuan Wharf.

(Three Robberies, Loss of Ten Thousand Yuan) The Pirates' Intention to Rob the Yu Shun Steamer Was Based on the Rumors in Guangdong That Three Wealthy People Were Taking The Ship to Shanghai With a Large Amount of Money. Therefore, After Launching the Attack, They Only Focused on Valuables and Not on Goods. There Were 150 Passengers and 3,132 Pieces of Cargo On The Ship. The Passengers' Valuables Could Not Be Avoided, and Only Two Boxes of Silverware (Table Settings) Were Taken From the Cargo. Because They Did Not Find a Large Amount of Money, They Were Unsatisfied, So They Involved the Crew, Creating a New Record in Maritime Robbery History. According to the Crew Who Witnessed It, The Robbery Was Divided Into Three Stages: The First Time Was for Money, the Second Time Was for Clothes, and the Third Time Was a Thorough Search, Even the Bedding Was Taken. The Total Loss, Excluding the Passengers, Was 400 Yuan for Ship Owner Huang Hongqian, 1,200 Yuan for the Chief Officer, Englishman Nelson, Approximately One Hundred Yuan for The Three Compardores Jin Chunxun, and Five of the Chief Officer's Six Pairs of Leather Shoes Were Gone. The Remaining Pair Was Spared Because They Were Old and Broken. The Total Loss Was Approximately 10,000 Yuan.

(Sixteen Pirates Escaped to Haifeng) According to The Yu Shun Steamer's Second Mate Shen Quanhai, There Were a Total of Sixteen Pirates. The Pirate Leader Was a Cripple, Said to Be The One Who Robbed The Guangli Steamer Previously. He Hid His Pistol In His Leggings. The Shantou Police Paid Attention to The Luggage, But Did Not Check His Body, So He Was Able to Get On The Ship. Most of The Pirates Were Wearing Blue and Black Silk Cloth Shirts and Pants, and There Were Approximately Ten Guns. Because They Stole and Robbed Without Firing and Injuring Anyone, Chief Officer Nelson, Helmsman Xin Jincai, and The Others of Us Were Robbed and Humiliated. The Pirates Wanted to Force Us to Hand Over Firearms, But We Did Not Carry Self-Defense Pistols. Most of The Pirates Spoke The Chaozhou Dialect, But Some Spoke The Ningbo Dialect. The Pirate Leader Was A Lame Man Close to Forty Years Old, Extremely Fierce. After Launching The Robbery at 9:05 PM That Night, He Forced The Engine Room to Sail to Haifeng. At Midnight, He Ordered The Stewards to Prepare Meals. They Intercepted Ships Three Times Along The Way, Firing Two Shots. At Noon On The First, They Intercepted a Fishing Boat For The Third Time. In Less Than An Hour, They Transferred to The Boat and Escaped to Honghai Bay. Haifeng Was Originally a Place Where Pirates Gathered. Da'ao Bay Is Their Main Nest, and Honghai Bay Is Just a Small Den.

(The Accountant and Crew Are Suspected of Colluding With Bandits) Later, The Reporter Met With The Yu Shun Steamer's First Mate Chen Bangda At The China Merchants Bureau. According to Him, The Total Loss of The Yu Shun Steamer Was Estimated at 10,000 Yuan. After The Pirates Arrived at Honghai Bay, They Escaped Towards Nuomo Mountain (Namoai). Of The Three Kidnapped People, One Was Huang Zanmin, a Staff Member of The Comprador's Office (Also Known as Huang Jiayan), From Chongming. The Other Two Were Mo Guocui, a Military Training Student From Yushan Middle School, and Shen Zhenxin, From Guangdong Provincial First Middle School, Who Were Both Coming to Shanghai and Then Going to Peiping to Transfer Schools. Their Whereabouts Are Still Unknown. All Crew Members Arrested in Shantou Are Currently Being Detained in Shantou for Interrogation. Of The Passengers Coming to Shanghai Today, Approximately Fifty Arrived in Shanghai, With Some Returning to Shantou. The Head Office Temporarily Issued Subsistence Allowances to The Crew Who Were Robbed. Yu Shun Has Decided to Resume Normal Operations to Qingdao On The Morning of The 9th.

(No One Dared to Claim The Thousand-Yuan Check) During This Pirate Robbery of The Yu Shun Steamer, A Check For 1,700 Yuan Was Found in Someone's Suitcase While Robbing The Passengers' Luggage. At That Time, All The Passengers Were Locked Together in The Main Dining Room. When The Pirates Obtained This Check, They Did Not Know Whose It Was. Therefore, They Pretended to Ask The Passengers, Willing to Return The Check. After Asking For a Long Time, The Owner Did Not Come Forward to Claim It, So They Tore It to Pieces In Anger and Threw It Into The Sea. It Was Later Found That The Check Belonged to Lu Jianhua, a Merchant From Fujian. He Did Not Dare to Claim It Because He Was Afraid That The Pirates Would Know That He Had Money and Take Him Along, Extorting a Large Sum. He Was Indeed Wise.

(China Merchants Bureau Reforms Business System) Ship Owner Huang Hongqian Arrived in Shanghai and Reported the Incident to Liu Hongsheng, General Manager of the China Merchants Bureau, and Zhao Yuntai, Head of the Shipping Department. The Crew's Losses Will Be Compensated After the Situation Is Clarified. Therefore, Yu Shun Is Still Scheduled to Sail to Qingdao to Unload Goods on the 9th as Usual. However, Liu Hongsheng Believes That This Incident Could Not Be Prevented, Which Was Due to the Deficiencies in the Business System. He Is Determined to Abolish the Comprador System, and the Stewards and Laborers Will Be Employed by the Bureau Itself, Similar to the Puan and Xinming Cases, in Order to Avoid Unexpected Events. On the One Hand, He Is Actively Seeking Preventive Measures, Which Are Currently Being Discussed and Handled by the Ministry of Communications. As for the Three Kidnapped People, Because It Is Impossible to Contact Them for the Time Being, and The China Merchants Bureau Has Not Been Able to Send Personnel to Contact Them on Behalf of The Passengers, Their Whereabouts Are Still Unknown.

County Government Officials Issue Instructions Busily 90

The Shanghai County Government Found That the Outstanding Taxes From Each District Were Still Huge, Especially in the Second District. Therefore, It Believed That the Tax Collector of That District, Zhu Jinsheng, Was Extremely Negligent. Therefore, He Was Arrested and Ordered to Recover the Taxes. Later, He Was Released on Bail Due to Illness While in Custody. Now, the County Government Believes That the Annual Taxes Should Be Collected From the First Day of This Month. Therefore, It Summoned Tax Collectors From Each District Yesterday and Issued Instructions. In Addition to Instructing Them on the Correct Amount of Taxes to Be Collected, It Also Told the Officials That, "Now Is the Time When the Province and County Are in Financial Difficulty. You Should Handle Your Duties Seriously and Not Be As Negligent As Before. As for the Outstanding Taxes From the Winter Season, You Should Urge Collection As Soon As Possible and Hand Them Over in Full." The Officials All Complied With the Instructions and Left.

Villagers Gather to Discuss Preventing the Opening of the Pu Hui Pond Dam 91

(Because It Does Not Follow the Original Plan of Six Zhang Wide at the River Surface, Two Zhang Wide at the River Bottom)

(Eight Chi Deep at the River Bottom)

Since the Shanghai West Pu Hui Pond Was Contracted Out by the Municipal Bureau of Public Works for Dredging in Sections, Sections 1 and 2 Have Been Completed. Sections 3, 4, and 5 Were Originally Scheduled to Be Inspected and Accepted the Day Before Yesterday. Later, Because All the Merchants and Residents of Hongqiao Town Requested the Bureau of Public Works to Order the Contractor, Shen Rongji, to Redredge According to the Original Size and Depth, in Order to Benefit Navigation and Achieve Complete Success, Now It Is Learned That the Contractor, Shen Rongji, Only Slightly Removed the Silt From the River Bottom and Dumped It on Both Sides of the Riverbank, Still Not Following the Original Plan of Six Zhang Wide at the River Surface, Two Zhang Wide at the River Bottom, and Eight Chi Deep at the River Bottom. Moreover, He Reduced the Earthwork and Tried to Deceptively Report to the Higher Authorities to Send Personnel to Inspect and Accept It, Hoping to Sell It Off. This Was Discovered by the Residents Along the River, Who Opposed It One After Another, Inviting Farmers to Discuss Preventing the Opening of the Dam. After Discussion, It Was Decided That (1) People Should Be Sent to Guard the Dam Foundation to Prevent Secret Opening (2) The Water From Each Tributary River Should Be Filled (3) The Bureau of Public Works Should Be Requested to Order the Contractor to Redredge (4) Before Redredging, Illegal Inspection and Acceptance Should Not Be Allowed.

Page 11

Singapore Restricts the Entry of Chinese

Shipping Companies Dare Not Sell Tickets 92

Since Mexico Expelled Overseas Chinese and Japan Banned Chinese Laborers From Entering the Country, Colonies of Various Countries Have Also Repeatedly Refused Entry to Our Compatriots. In This Vast World, There Is No Place for Our Chinese People to Stand. Now Singapore Is Said to Restrict the Entry of Chinese.

(Limiting the Number of Entries) British Singapore Has the Largest Number of Overseas Chinese Businessmen in Our Country, and Many Industries Are Operated by Chinese. There Has Never Been a Limit on Our Overseas Chinese Going to Singapore. Every Year, No Less Than 100,000 Overseas Chinese From Fujian and Guangdong Provinces Travel Back and Forth. Unexpectedly, the Singapore Authorities Suddenly Limited the Number of Chinese Entering the Country and Issued Residence Permits to Those Who Have Lived in Singapore for a Long Time. Without This Certificate, They Will Be Rejected for Being Over Quota and Not Allowed to Land. Recently, Many Batches of People Who Have Been Rejected and Sent Back Have Already Been Sent Back.

(Overseas Chinese Going to Singapore Are Blocked) The Italian Postal Shipping Company's Kang Tuo Fan Te Steamer, Which Was Going From Shanghai to Europe on Its Regular Route, Had Forty-Nine Chinese Passengers, Who Were Taking the Ship From Shanghai and Hong Kong to Singapore. Most of These Chinese Were Going for Business, or Were Originally Residing in Singapore, Returning Home for Business, and Then Going Back. When the Ship Arrived in Singapore, the Colonial Authorities Prohibited This Batch of Chinese From Entering the Country, Claiming That the Quota of Overseas Chinese Arriving in Singapore Had Been Reached, and None Were Allowed to Land. Later, After the Italian Postal Company Repeatedly Negotiated With the Singapore Authorities and Presented the Residence Permits of the Chinese, After Several Disputes, They Finally Agreed to Be Accommodating Once, and in the Future, They Would Not Be Allowed to Carry Chinese to Singapore Again.

(Telegram to Stop Carrying Chinese) On July 24, the Singapore Italian Postal Company Specially Sent a Telegram to Shanghai, Informing the Shanghai Branch That the Singapore Authorities Were Suppressing the Entry of Chinese and Limiting the Number of People. The Quota Was Now Full, and No More Chinese Were Allowed to Arrive in Singapore. Shanghai Was Ordered to Stop Selling Tickets to Chinese Going to Singapore. If They Disobeyed the Order and Carried Them, in Addition to Being Prohibited From Landing, the Colonial Government Would Also Punish the Shipping Company. After This Telegram Arrived in Shanghai, There Were Major Obstacles for Chinese Taking Ships to Singapore.

(Difficulty Purchasing Tickets) After This Suppression Order Arrived in Shanghai, It Has Become Difficult for Chinese in Shanghai to Go to Singapore. Shipping Companies Are Afraid to Sell Tickets Rashly. If Passengers Insist on Buying Tickets, Unless They Prepay 1,000 Singapore Dollars to Be Used as a Fine When Prohibited From Landing, There Is No Other Way. Yesterday, the Manager of the Italian Postal Company Specially Went to the British Consulate in This Port to Ask Whether Chinese Could Be Allowed to Go to Singapore. On the One Hand, Only Those With Residence Permits Were Allowed to Sell Tickets to Singapore, But Only One or Two People Were Allowed, and More Would Result in Stopping Sales.

The Settlement of Post-Disaster Issues of the Goutan Steamer's Workers Has Been Successfully Resolved 93

The Preparatory Committee for the China Seamen's Union Formulated Measures That Were Approved by an Order From the Ministry of Communications The Long-Pending Issue of the Goutan Steamer's Workers' Post-Disaster Issues Has Been Negotiated by the Preparatory Committee of the China Seamen's Union in Various Ways. On the 29th and 31st of Last Month, It Convened the China Merchants Bureau to Comply With the Intentions of the Ministry of Communications and Made Concrete Consultations Within the Scope of Not Conflicting With National Laws and Regulations. Subsequently, the Preparatory Committee Formulated Six Post-Disaster Measures and Submitted Them to the Ministry of Communications for Approval. It Has Just Been Learned That These Measures Were Highly Commended by the Ministry. The Committee Received Order No. 1445 From the Ministry of Communications Yesterday, and Immediately Informed the China Merchants Bureau to Comply With It. It Also Notified All Family Members and Surviving Workers That Certificates Issued by the Association Were Required to Receive Compensation, Otherwise, They Would Not Be Valid, in Order to Show Solemnity and Prevent Impersonation. The Details Are Recorded Below:

(Notice to Family Members) Regarding the Post-Disaster Measures for the Goutan Steamer's Workers and Deceased Family Members, This Association Has Formulated Measures and Submitted Them to the Ministry of Communications for Approval. It Is Estimated That Each Deceased Family Member Will Receive a Compensation of Six Hundred and Sixty Yuan, Including All Losses, Burial Expenses, and Other Expenses. Each Deceased Worker Will Receive Compensation of One Hundred and Sixty Yuan, Including All Property and Loss of Employment. All Family Members Who Have Received a Portion of the Compensation From the China Merchants Bureau Are Requested to Come to the Association to Re-Register in Order to Receive the Compensation Certificate and Hold It to the China Merchants Bureau to Receive the Compensation That Is Due. All Family Members and Workers Who Have Not Received It Should Register at the Post-Disaster Association, Which Will Be Collected and Reported Again Before Issuing It. However, for the Sake of Caution, No Compensation Can Be Received From the Bureau Without a Compensation Certificate Issued by This Association. This Is Specially Notified.

(Nuclear Instructions From Ministry of Communications) The Measures Submitted Are Generally Appropriate. They Are Revised Separately as Follows: (1) The Compensation for the Family Members of Sailors Who Died While Performing Ship Duties Should Be Handled in Accordance With the Provisions of Article 67 of the Maritime Law, But If Their Annual Wages Are Less Than 660 Yuan, They Should Be Paid According to 660 Yuan, Including All Losses, Burial Expenses, and Other Expenses. (2) Surviving Sailors Should Be Given a Loss Fee of 160 Yuan, Including All Property and Loss of Employment. (3) When the Bureau Has Vacancies for Deceased Sailors, They Should Be Given Priority for Recruitment.
