It Notified Yang Hengzhen to Revoke the Permit Issued by the Bureau to Undertake the Loading and Unloading of Goods at the Station, and the 10,000 Yuan Deposit Previously Paid by the Contractor Was Returned in Full. The Important Documents Published by the Road Bureau Are Recorded As Follows:

(Ministry of Railways' Instructions) The Ministry of Railways' Instructions, General Word No. 6017, Are Issued for Action. It Has Been Found That the Case of the Dispute Among the Loading and Unloading Workers of the Mai Gen Road Freight Station of the Road Has Been Settled by the Ministry in Consultation With the Central Mass Movement Guidance Committee, and the Provisional Rules of the Loading and Unloading Workers' Office of the Station Have Been Established. In Addition to Sending the Provisional Rules to the Central Mass Movement Guidance Committee for Review, It Is Ordered That a Copy of the Provisional Rules Be Issued to You for Compliance With and Report to the Ministry for Consideration. This Order.

(Road Bureau's Announcement) For Announcement, It Has Been Found That This Bureau Revoked the Loading and Unloading Workers' Cooperative of the Mai Gen Road Freight Station in Accordance With Article 26 of the Trial Regulations of the Cooperative, and Approved Yang Hengzhen to Undertake the Loading and Unloading of Goods at the Station in Accordance With the Measures for Undertaking the Loading and Unloading of Railway Goods Promulgated by the Ministry of Railways. Later, Disputes Arose, and This Bureau Reported to the Ministry of Railways, Consulting With the Central Party Headquarters Mass Movement Guidance Committee for Instructions and Awaiting Resolution. It Has Now Received Instructions From the Ministry of Railways and the Central Party Headquarters Mass Movement Guidance Committee to Allow the Loading and Unloading Workers of the Station to Form the Mai Gen Road Freight Station Loading and Unloading Workers' Office, Requesting to Undertake the Loading and Unloading of Goods at the Mai Gen Road Freight Station in Accordance With the Measures for Undertaking the Loading and Unloading of Railway Goods Promulgated by the Ministry of Railways and to Sign a Contract. The Ministry of Railways Has Appointed Committee Members Yang Ge and Guo Zhongxing, and the Central Party Headquarters Mass Movement Guidance Committee Has Appointed Comrade Li Renzhu to Come to the Road to Guide and Handle It. In Addition to Notifying Yang Hengzhen to Revoke the Previously Issued Permit to Undertake the Loading and Unloading of Goods at the Station, the 15 Provisional Rules of the Mai Gen Road Freight Station Loading and Unloading Workers' Office Are Announced for Public Knowledge. The Loading and Unloading Workers of the Station Should Comply With the Provisions of the Rules and Handle the Necessary Procedures Under the Guidance of the Commissioners Specially Appointed by the Central Party Headquarters Mass Movement Guidance Committee and the Ministry of Railways. This Is of Utmost Importance. This Announcement.

(Provisional Rules) Provisional Rules of the Mai Gen Road Freight Station Loading and Unloading Workers' Office, (Article 1) In Order to Undertake the Loading and Unloading of Railway Goods at the Mai Gen Road Freight Station of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways, With the Approval of the Road Bureau, the Loading and Unloading Workers of the Station May Organize the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways Mai Gen Road Freight Station Loading and Unloading Workers' Office (Hereinafter Referred to As the Office)) Article 2 (The Loading and Unloading Workers of the Office Must Comply With the Following Provisions (1) Have Been Registered and Approved by the Road Bureau and Received a Number Plate Issued by the Road Bureau (2) Be Physically Strong and Able to Undertake Loading and Unloading Work (3) Be Upright in Conduct and Have No Bad Habits (4) Have Not Been Punished by Dismissal by the Road Bureau) (Article 3 (The Office Shall Have Two Chief Class Leaders. In Order to Facilitate the Work, All the Loading and Unloading Workers Shall Be Divided Into Several Classes, Each Class Shall Have One Class Leader, and the Office Shall Appoint One to Three Employees As Appropriate, (Article 4) In Addition to Complying With the Provisions of Article 2, the Chief Class Leader and Class Leaders Must Comply With the Following Provisions, (1) Be Able to Manage and Command the Loading and Unloading Workers (2) Have Considerable Credibility Among Customers, Merchants, and Workers of the Road Bureau, (Article 5) The Chief Class Leader Shall Be in Charge of All Affairs of the Office, the Class Leader Shall Be in Charge of All Affairs of His Class According to the Order of the Chief Class Leader, and the Employees Shall Be in Charge of the Accounts and Miscellaneous Matters of the Office According to the Order of the Chief Class Leader, (Article 6) The Chief Class Leader Shall Be Elected by All the Loading and Unloading Workers, and the Class Leaders Shall Be Elected by the Loading and Unloading Workers of Each Class. After the Election, a List of Names, Votes, and Election Conditions Shall Be Prepared and Submitted to the Road Bureau for Approval and Filing,) Article 7 (The Office Shall Be Represented by the Chief Class Leader and Shall Request the Road Bureau to Undertake the Loading and Unloading of Railway Goods at the Mai Gen Road Freight Station and Sign a Contract in Accordance With the Measures for Undertaking the Loading and Unloading of Railway Goods Promulgated by the Ministry of Railways (Article 8) The Office's Office Location Must Be Located Within the Scope of the Mai Gen Road Freight Station (Article 9) One-Tenth of the Loading and Unloading Fee Shall Be Taken Out As the Office's Expenses and Public Accumulation Fund, But the Number of Expenses Shall Not Exceed 80% of the Total Amount Taken Out. The Expenses Shall Include the Salaries of the Chief Class Leader, the Class Leaders, and the Employees, As Well As All Miscellaneous Expenses. The Public Accumulation Fund Shall Be Used Exclusively for the Public Welfare of All the Workers in the Office, and the Measures for Its Management Shall Be Formulated Separately, (Article 10) The Office Shall Be Subject to the Supervision and Command of the Road Bureau, (Article 11) If the Class Leader and the Loading and Unloading Workers Have Any of the Following Circumstances, the Road Bureau May Order the Chief Class Leader to Punish or Dismiss Them Separately With the Approval of the Chief Class Leader, (1) Violating Regulations (2) Found to Be Inconsistent With the Provisions of Articles 2 and 4 (3) Extorting Customers, (Article 12) If the Chief Class Leader Has Any of the Following Circumstances, the Road Bureau May Impose Punishment, Revoke His Qualifications As Chief Class Leader, or Dismiss Him As Appropriate (1) Violating Regulations, (2) Found to Be Inconsistent With the Provisions of Articles 2 and 4, (2) Extorting Customers, Exploiting Workers, and Other Illegal Activities. If the Chief Class Leader's Qualifications Are Revoked or He Is Dismissed, He May Be Re-Elected by All the Workers,) Article 13 (If Any of the Following Circumstances Occurs, the Road Bureau May Revoke the Contract and Dissolve the Office, (1) Failing to Perform the Contract (2) Endangering Traffic and Obstructing Railway Operations (3) During the Validity Period of the Contract, the Chief Class Leader Is Revoked More Than Three Times by the Road Bureau (Article 14) These Provisional Rules Shall Take Effect From the Date of Signing of the Contract (Article 15) The Implementation and Abolition of These Provisional Rules Shall Be Submitted by the Road Bureau to the Ministry of Railways for Approval and Filing (Revoking the Undertaking)

Road Administration and Other Announcements and Letters to the

Special Party Headquarters of the Two Roads, the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs, the Public Security Bureau, and the Security Office for Reference and Reply to the Ministry of Railways for Compliance. Members Yang and Lin have a long history with the seamen and possess a spirit of sacrifice for the revolution. In the future, they should work to unite the seamen internally and relieve their suffering, and so on.

He hopes that everyone will pay attention to this opportunity.

The organization of the Chinese Seamen's Union is vast, and its undertakings are complex. We must work hard with a spirit of sacrifice. The points we should strive for in the future are: 1. To unite the seamen internally to seek our own liberation; 2. To develop the national shipping industry and reclaim the right to navigate inland rivers; 3. To improve the treatment of seamen as much as possible without hindering the shipping industry itself."

Construction Commission Continues to Issue Six Million in Electrical Bonds 96

(Issuance methods have been submitted to the Executive Yuan for review) (Secured by the Capital Qishuyan Power Plant) Three principles have been decided for use and distribution The National Government Construction Commission previously issued long-term bonds of 1.5 million yuan and short-term bonds of 2.5 million yuan to develop the Capital and Qishuyan power plants. It is now learned that although state-owned electrical enterprises have made great progress in recent years, they are constrained by economic difficulties, and some projects that should be undertaken have not been implemented. To gradually implement the government's construction plan, the commission plans to continue issuing bonds worth 6 million yuan. According to sources in the city's banking sector, the bond issuance methods have been detailed by the commission and submitted to the Executive Yuan for review, after which they will be announced. The face value of the bonds will be 1,000 yuan and 10,000 yuan, with an annual interest rate of 6%. Interest will be paid on June 30th and October 31st each year, secured by the address, buildings, machinery, and profits of the Capital and Qishuyan power plants. The principles for use and distribution have been determined as: 1. Opening the Huainan Power Plant, as the Construction Commission has a coal mine nearby that will require a large amount of electricity when developed on a large scale in the future, so it has been decided to build a power plant there to meet the needs. 2. Expanding the Qishuyan Power Plant by purchasing additional generators, increasing electricity production, and promoting small-scale electricity businesses. 3. Reorganizing the Capital Electric Light Plant by extending power lines as much as possible so that electricity can circulate everywhere.

One-Two-Eight Memorial Hall Scheduled to Open on the 10th 97

Meaning in the oil painting Songhu Garrison Commander Dai Ji, to commemorate the 19th Route Army's resistance against the Japanese in Shanghai and Songhu, specially allocated 8,000 yuan from the Ministry of Military Affairs several months ago to convert the original dining hall on the right side of the ministry into the One-Two-Eight Memorial Hall. A garden called the One-Two-Eight Garden was built around the hall, with a pavilion in the center called the One-Two-Eight Memorial Pavilion. A stone tablet was erected behind the hall, engraved with a commemorative text, signed by Dai, for eternal commemoration. Inside the hall, on the front wall, is a very large oil painting, with the Zhabei Commercial Press and the Zilai Pavilion as the background. In the front line is the solemn line of our army, and in the rear are enemy planes flying and dropping bombs, with smoke and fire covering the sky, truly inspiring people to reflect and strive. It is now learned that the oil painting has been completed, and Commander Dai has specifically scheduled the inauguration ceremony for the 10th of this month, when there will be a grand occasion.

Taxpayers' Association Sends Another Letter to the Public Works Department, Urging the Telephone Company to Respect Public Opinion 98

Quickly abolish the five-cent call fee to facilitate traffic The abolition of the five-cent call fee for Chinese concessions has been eagerly awaited by the general public. However, although the Shanghai Telephone Bureau has expressed its intention to abolish it automatically, the Shanghai Telephone Company has still failed to adapt to the trend. The Chinese Taxpayers' Association of the Public Concession yesterday urged the Public Works Department again on this matter, requesting the company to respect public opinion, and replied to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce. The original letter is recorded below:

(Reply to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce) In reply to your association's letter No. 3246 of August 3rd, regarding the unanimous mobilization to urge the Shanghai Telephone Company to follow the Shanghai Telephone Bureau in abolishing the call fee between the area under the jurisdiction of the Municipal Public Security Bureau and the Special Zone. We have received this. The purpose of a telephone is to facilitate traffic. Within the same city area, although the managing organization may be allowed to be more than two, restricting communication between users fails to fully realize its effectiveness. It is said that abolishing the five-cent call fee between the area under the jurisdiction of the Municipal Public Security Bureau and the Special Zone will increase the burden on users who do not need this type of call fee, which is unfair. This is an untenable argument. May we ask whether the number of times a user with the same usage fee uses the telephone is the same? This association believes that abolishing this call fee will further promote fairness and convenience among users. It is said that those who refuse to abolish this call fee are actually doing so for private gain and are using the argument that unequal treatment will occur among users as a pretext. This association does not believe it. It concerns the convenience of traffic and the necessity of developing municipal administration. We hereby request your bureau to quickly order the Shanghai Telephone Company to abolish the aforementioned five-cent call fee to show respect for the purpose of operating a telephone franchise. We have now received the above. In addition to sending another letter to the Public Works Department urging them to order the Shanghai Telephone Company to implement it quickly, we hereby reply for your information. To the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce.

(Letter to the Public Works Department) We previously sent a letter on July 15th regarding facilitating telephone traffic, requesting your bureau to quickly order the Shanghai Telephone Company to abolish the five-cent call fee for calls between the North and South Municipalities to show respect for the purpose of operating a franchise. We have not yet received a reply, which is greatly anticipated. Now that the Shanghai Telephone Bureau has been approved to implement it, we believe that your bureau will be able to respect public opinion and facilitate traffic, not falling behind others. As we have not yet received a reply informing us of the handling situation, we hereby send another letter, hoping that you will quickly order the matter to be handled. To the General Manager of the Shanghai Public Concession Public Works Department.

Resolution of Dispute Over Tobacco and Alcohol Licenses 99

The Shanghai Municipal Tobacco, Alcohol, and Sauce Association previously stated that Director Ding Xie (Jin Sheng) of the Tobacco and Alcohol License Tax Collection Office, due to taking on the responsibility of collecting this tax, had increased the quota, making the burden already heavy. It was proposed to change the two-yuan license for the tobacco and alcohol industries to four yuan, with similar increases for others, otherwise, the losses would be severe. After repeated consultations with the leaders of the two industries, a decision could not be reached. The tax side agreed to allow members to be flexible as appropriate. As a result of negotiations between the two sides, payment will still be made according to the usual practice. The Tonghui notified members that the dispute had been resolved from now on, and all shops should entrust the association to pay the autumn licenses on their behalf. Thirty-six shops were obstructed and instructed to add more. The association again notified member shops not to start disputes again. Upon questioning the person in charge of the association, yesterday, Zhang Dalian of the Sauce and Alcohol Industry Association sent representative Qian Dousheng to the South Railway Station License Tax Office at 10:00 AM, together with Qian Wenda and Chen Kunxian, the director and deputy director of the Shanghai South Office of the Tobacco Industry Association, for further negotiations. Directors Chen and Cheng of the office extended a meeting. Licenses for members will still be collected according to the regulations. Those who have been paid on behalf of the association will also be treated accordingly. If there are any alterations or mismatched grades, the association is requested to assist in dispatching personnel for investigation and persuasion. Non-members should not be accepted. The representatives then took their leave. The repeated disputes were completely resolved.

Shanghai-Ningbo-Suzhou Tobacco and Alcohol Joint Association Telegraphs Request to Dismiss the Chief of the Shangbao Branch Bureau 100

The New Voice News Agency reports that the Shanghai-Ningbo-Suzhou Tobacco and Alcohol Industry Association yesterday telegraphed the Ministry of Finance's Taxation Department and the Director of the Jiangsu Stamp Tobacco and Alcohol Tax Bureau, stating that on the 6th of this month, a letter from the Shanghai Shaoxing Wine Industry Association stated that, according to the previous Jiangsu Public Monopoly Regulations, all Shaoxing wine transported from Zhejiang and sold in other provinces should be reported to the Shanghai collection agency, specifying the quantity, and after the goods and documents are verified to be consistent, a stamp should be affixed for release, without obstruction. It is now reported by Pan Yangsheng of De Tai Chang Shaoxing Wine Shop that on July 17th, 500 jars of Beijing-grade Jia Da Shaoxing wine were transported from Zhejiang and sold in Beiping. According to the regulations, it should still be

reported to the Shangbao Tobacco and Alcohol Tax Branch Bureau, and after the goods and documents are verified to be consistent, a stamp should be affixed for release, which is the proper procedure. However, the newly appointed Chief of the Shangbao Branch Bureau, Huang Yong (Huang Yuming), stated that according to the new tax regulations promulgated by the Ministry of Finance on July 1st, wine passing through the area must pay the new tax, otherwise, the goods would be confiscated and punished. Yangsheng argued with reason, but to no avail. The branch bureau detained all the wine declared to the customs and waiting to be loaded onto a sea vessel, causing delays and considerable losses. The merchant had no choice but to reluctantly pay the new tax of 3.4 cents per jar on the 18th, totaling 170 yuan. Furthermore, it was reported by Dong Sheng Qing Wine Shop that 70 jars of Jia Da wine transported from Shaoxing to Hou Sheng Shop in Dalian were also

taxed 16.8 yuan, and the Zhejiang tax票was confiscated, and a guarantee was provided. The details were reported to the association, and Jin Yunjie, a standing committee member, replied that according to the new regulations,

this type of wine does not require supplementary tax. If it is said that supplementary tax can be paid along the way, then the new tax is similar to a disguised likin tax. However, the Shangbao area has a wide market, ranking first in Jiangsu Province. It is assumed that the director, being a high-ranking official, must be familiar with the new regulations and would not make any mistakes. However, after checking Article 14 of the Ministry's regulations, there is no need to pay supplementary tax. It is feared that there are other detailed rules specifying the supplementary tax regulations, which are unknown. After requesting the department and bureau to explain clearly, a reply will be given. Soon after, Jin Changwu reviewed the situation and stated that only Article 14 of the new regulations

could be followed, and there are no other detailed rules for supplementary tax, and so on. It is found that Huang Yong, Chief of the Shangbao Branch Bureau, who holds the power of monopoly, is not familiar with the regulations and uses fraudulent means, relying on his power to implement coercion. This is enough to prove that he is imposing excessive taxes and levies, which cannot be denied. Merchants are difficult to endure. If the joint association is not requested to appeal to the Taxation Department and provincial authorities on behalf of the merchants, this tax revenue will be completely defrauded. Therefore, a factual report is submitted, requesting you to send a letter to the joint association, which will forward it to the Ministry of Finance's Taxation Department and the Jiangsu Stamp Tobacco and Alcohol Tax Bureau for review to ascertain the truth, quickly refund the illegally levied tax, and dismiss and punish the Chief of the Bureau, Huang Yong, who illegally levies taxes, to rectify official conduct and ensure fairness. The report from the association also stated that, after reviewing the information, we found that the regulations clearly stipulate that wine transported from the place of origin to other provinces should be inspected and released without levying tax. The bureau chief holds a high position and should not act so ignorantly. Furthermore, withholding items requires special provisions according to the law. Now, at the time of reforming tax rates, he is undermining the Ministry's regulations, intensifying his actions, and levying taxes without authorization, violating criminal law. This is truly detrimental to official integrity. Upon receiving the report, it was found that, regardless of the new or old system, the inspection and release of Shaoxing wine passing through the area is required. At the beginning of the implementation of the new tax, the chief of the branch bureau dared to violate the regulations and extort taxes, giving others an excuse, and hindering the new policy. Whether this is meritorious or a mistake is clear to all. If he is not severely punished, how can those who follow suit be deterred? According to the previous letter, it is appropriate to telegraph this. We hope that you will review and approve this, quickly send personnel to investigate and handle the matter, and investigate the matter impartially, to warn those who are greedy and to reassure honest merchants. We also ask for instructions to be given so that we can inform you, and we will be extremely grateful. Joint Association of Shanghai-Ningbo-Suzhou Alcohol Industry Association, Chairman Zhang Dalian, Standing Committee Members Jin Yunjie, Jin Jia, Dai Zhuoan, Chen Weiwen, Joint Association of Shanghai-Ningbo-Suzhou Tobacco Industry Association, Chairman Chen Liangyu, etc.

(Twelve people escorted from Tianjin to Shanghai were interrogated yesterday) (The backgrounds of the bandits are diverse, including principals and prostitutes) They committed many crimes in Shanghai and are currently under investigation. Geng Huatang, a notorious kidnapper from Jinan, is 58 years old this year. He previously served as a division commander. After the Jiazi year Jiang-Zhe war, Geng left his post and lived in the French Concession. Due to financial difficulties, he engaged in kidnapping. Because Geng could not establish himself in Shanghai, he fled to Tianjin, often secretly contacting his accomplices in Shanghai, still engaged in his old business, and after obtaining funds, he fled back to Tianjin.

The details have been recorded in previous reports. After the questioning, police lawyer Yuan Jiahuang stood up and stated the case, saying that the defendants were arrested in Tianjin on the 25th of last month for kidnapping and brought to Shanghai on the 5th of this month. The police stated that the defendants had committed many crimes, and the case was complex and had not yet been investigated. Police Officer Bai Linguang Commits Suicide 105

(Due to both family troubles and illness)

His suicide note stated the reasons as follows: Bai Linguang, a police officer from the Sanjing Police Station of the Second Branch of the Third District in Pudong, was on guard at the entrance of the station from 0:00 AM to 3:00 AM yesterday morning. However, around 2:30 AM, in the dead of night, the officer suddenly took off the rifle he was carrying, pointed the muzzle at his lower jaw, pulled the trigger, and shot himself. With a loud bang, the bullet entered from the lower left jaw and exited from the left side of the brain, creating a large hole from the teeth to the temples. He collapsed on the empty ground next to the police station. The police chief, Wang Zhaolin, heard the sound and rushed out of bed to investigate. He saw the officer lying on the ground with his head facing south and feet facing north, moaning and twisting, but not yet dead. He immediately sent officers to take him to the hospital for treatment. However, due to the severity of the injury, he died midway and was taken back to the station. The incident was reported to the Second Branch for verification. The director of the branch received the report and immediately sent Inspector Yu Zuyao to the entrance of the station to investigate. It was learned that when the deceased fell to the ground, the rifle was close to his body, and the trigger seemed to have been activated by his right toe. Upon searching the deceased's body, two suicide notes were found. The tone of the notes indicated that he intended to retire and return home due to illness, but he felt ashamed to face people, so he conceived the idea of ending his life. Inspector Yu took the notes back to the station and reported to the director, who instructed the local bailiff, Ma Xichuan, to report to the local court, which sent prosecutor Du Pu to the scene to verify that the officer had indeed committed suicide by shooting himself. The body was handed over to the station to prepare a coffin for burial. It is said that the deceased was 28 years old and a native of Beiping. He was transferred from Beiping after the Shanghai war. He suffered from neurasthenia and was often ill. This sudden suicide was unexpected by others. His suicide notes are recorded below: 1. When I left home, it was because my newlywed wife of less than two years had passed away. After my wife died, my parents and siblings-in-law had disagreements and argued and fought all day long. I got sick in anger for more than two months. When I was about 70% or 80% recovered, I came to Shanghai and have been here for more than a year, not sending a single cent home. Thinking that if I am not sick now, I would have no choice but to apply for a long vacation. But then I thought about the things at home. Going home now would be like becoming a disabled person. How would I have the face to see my parents and neighbors? So yesterday I went to Shanghai to cheer myself up for a day. After returning to the station, I thought about it and developed the idea of ending my life. I wanted to do it half a day ago (the meaning of these numbers is unclear). After walking around for a week with the gun, I thought again about how the police chief treats people like a Buddha, and my colleagues have no enemies or hatred. So I shot myself and died, without any complaints. Handwritten by Bai Linguang. 2. Dear Police Chief, I am truly sorry for you. I am causing you trouble. I will thank you in the next life. Because there is a military uniform paper, please investigate it. August 5th.

Resurrection from the Dead 108

) Already sent to the morgue ((Unexpectedly, his life was not destined to end)

On the 3rd of this month, near the Jiangwan train station, a man, approximately thirty years old, dressed in rags and resembling a beggar, collapsed on the road. A patrol officer from the Fifth Precinct, Fifth Sub-precinct, noticed him and promptly sent him to the Jiangwan Public Security Road Epidemic Hospital for treatment. The hospital doctor examined him, but the man had been silent since entering the hospital, so his name and place of origin remained unknown. Around 5 a.m. yesterday, his condition suddenly worsened, and efforts to save him were ineffective, resulting in his death. The hospital sent the body to the morgue to await preparation for burial, and simultaneously reported to the Fifth Sub-precinct, which instructed the local warden to request a forensic examination from the court. Unexpectedly, at that moment, the man suddenly revived and began breathing normally. The people in the hospital were greatly surprised upon seeing this and hurriedly reported to the Fifth Sub-precinct again. After a doctor's examination, it was confirmed that he had indeed come back to life. For a time, the news spread far and wide, and everyone regarded it as a miracle.

Account of the Reception Hosted by the United Securities Investment Company 114

The United Securities Investment Company at No. 570 Nanjing Road was founded by giants in Shanghai's financial circles. To facilitate business development and cater to Chinese investors, it established a Chinese Manager's Office at No. A-4 on the first floor at the intersection of Nanjing Road and Sichuan Road. Yesterday, it hosted a banquet at the Hongkou Hotel on North Sichuan Road, inviting prominent figures from the press and business circles, both Chinese and Western, to foster relationships. Attendees included Ma Yinliang from the Shen Bao, Wang Zhongwei, Yan Duhe, and Yu Kongwo from the Xinwen Bao, Zhang Zhuping, Pan Gongbi, and Xiong Shaohao from the Shishi Xinbao, Zeng Xubai, Chen Yaozhu, and Wang Jincheng from the Da Wan Bao, Wang Zhongji from the Shibao, Zhu Yitian from the Dalu Bao, and Zhao Jinqing from the business world, totaling over 200 people. The company's directors Zhu Boquan and Shi Boqun, Chinese Manager Yu Huidong, and Chinese Deputy Manager Wang Jia, etc., provided attentive hospitality. Around 7:00 PM, guests were seated, and Mr. Burke, Chairman of the company's board of directors, who is also the manager of the Bao Ke Foreign Firm and a director of the Lianli Film Company, presided over the event. During the banquet, Mr. Zhu Boquan stood up and delivered a speech, the text of which is as follows: "I am very honored to have you all grace us with your presence today, especially in this hot weather. Now, I have something to report to you and would like to ask for your guidance. The United Securities Investment Company is an investment institution serving the public. Its sole business is to promote securities through installment payments, without limiting the type of security, whether domestic or foreign, all are within the scope of our company's business. The first type we are promoting is the national credit bonds issued by France in 1920. Our company believes that these bonds have maintained their creditworthiness since their issuance and offer generous benefits, because in addition to the repayment of principal and interest, there are also substantial bonuses. The advantages are detailed in the purchase regulations printed by our company, so there is no need to repeat them here. In addition to France, lottery bonds have also been issued by Italy, Belgium, and Greece. In the future, our company will continue to introduce them to the public, giving them the opportunity to obtain large bonuses while making sound investments. In the past decade, the public has understood that saving is a good thing, and the financial industry has devised various methods to promote it. The most effective way to encourage saving is through lottery-based methods. However, the current lottery savings schemes inevitably have several drawbacks: 1) The term is too long, usually around ten years, and individuals may experience changes in their economic situation that prevent them from completing the full term; 2) The amount of the bonus is not fixed and often fluctuates depending on the number of savers; 3) The interest rate is too low, and some people who have paid installments for more than ten years only receive their own capital back. Those who win the lottery are naturally well-off, but those who do not win suffer too much. Now, the French national credit bonds sold by our company have the advantage of addressing the three drawbacks mentioned above: 1) Installment payments are only for 28 months, the term is very short, and there is little risk of being unable to continue payments halfway. Each month is only five yuan, averaging just over two jiao per day, which is truly easy to afford. Moreover, you receive a number, and after paying the first installment, you have the hope of winning the first prize; 2) Lottery drawings are held eight times a year, and each time, in addition to the first prize of 1 million French francs, there are 12 second to fifth prizes, all paid according to a fixed amount and never changing; 3) Those who win the lottery naturally get a satisfactory result, and those who do not win also receive an annual interest rate of 5% and can also share in a portion of the company's annual net profit. In short, subscribing to the French national credit bonds sold by our company provides both a savings opportunity and the hope of winning a large bonus, and you also enjoy a portion of the company's net profit. It can be said that it combines the advantages of various savings schemes and avoids the drawbacks of general lottery savings schemes. Today, all of you present are leaders of society, and your words carry great weight. On behalf of the company, I ask you to promote this vigorously, so that society knows that there is such an investment institution that serves the public. On the one hand, it can promote savings, and on the other hand, it can help our company develop its business. Both the public and private sectors will be very grateful to you all." Subsequently, Mr. Tang Zhixuan and Mr. Zhao Jinqing delivered replies. The company also hired a full Western dance troupe to perform various dances to entertain the guests. The event concluded at 10:00 PM. It is reported that the Chinese Manager's Office will officially open for business on the 10th of this month. Purchase regulations have been printed and are available for inquiries from all sectors.

Silk Weaving Factory Electricity Theft Case 119

Who should be held responsible? Zhu Fengchi, a native of Shaoxing and manager of the Yuanchang Silk Weaving Factory at No. 1 Binggang Lane, Tianbao Road, Zhabei, recently faced business difficulties and sold the factory's machinery to his fellow villager, Fang Jitu, to continue operations. The factory's looms were powered by electricity, so the monthly electricity bill was considerable. Chen Dexin, manager of the Zhabei Xianghua Electricity Company, found that the factory's electricity consumption had sharply decreased in the past two months and suspected electricity theft. He immediately sent staff to the factory and found that the lead seal on the meter had been tampered with. He then reported it to the relevant police station, and the police took both the former manager, Zhu Fengchi, and the current owner, Ji Jitu, into custody for questioning. Zhu Fengchi confessed that Jin Fanglan stole the electricity. Jin was subsequently arrested, and they were both sent to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for interrogation yesterday.

Shop Assistants Watching Gambling Together Leads to Death 120

(Patrolmen disperse (Near the Ming Mountain; Drowning (Recently, the weather has been extremely hot, with the Celsius thermometer constantly above 39 degrees. People are working hard during the day, and everyone is groaning with pain. They take advantage of their spare time in the evening to go out in groups to the Huangpu River or the wharf to cool off. Ma Shengzhen, a native of Nanjing, 38 years old, runs the Ma Shunxing paint shop opposite the Small World on Fuyou Road in the Chinese area. He employs Yang Akun (21 years old, from Wuxi), Gu Hongsheng (20 years old, from Changzhou), and Liu Mingshan (21 years old, from Nanjing) as shop assistants. They suffer from the heat during the day. After finishing work, they have nothing to do in the evening, so they go out to cool off. At 9:40 PM the night before last (the evening of the 6th), Yang, Gu, and Yang went out together to the Taikoo Wharf on the Bund in the French Concession to cool off. Three wharf loafers were gambling for fun at the wharf. Yang and the others stood by and watched. They were spotted by French Concession patrolmen No. 91, No. 106 (two Russian patrolmen), and No. 98 (a Chinese patrolman), who approached and beat and dispersed the loafers. The loafers had already been beaten and fled to the shore. The Russian patrolmen mistook Yang and the others for the loafers and beat them indiscriminately with batons without asking questions. At that time, only Gu Hongsheng ran ahead and escaped to the shore. Yang Akun and Liu Mingshan, panicked and ran in the wrong direction, and both accidentally fell into the river. Fortunately, Yang Akun was somewhat familiar with water and was able to climb to the shore. However, Liu Mingshan did not know how to swim and sank to the bottom of the river. He was drowned. After reaching the shore, Yang ran back to the shop and reported to the shop owner, Ma Shengzhen, and reported to the police station. He hired workers to search the wharf, but the body had not yet surfaced yesterday.

Assassins of Zhang Xinshan Sentenced 121

Zhang Xinshan, codenamed "Little Anhui," a 29-year-old Anhui native and Detective No. 62 of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau, residing on the rear building of No. 8 Zhenhua Lane, Malan Road, French Concession, was stabbed to death by his enemies at the entrance of Alley 1, Chongyi Lane, Malan Road, on the morning of the 8th of last month. Subsequently, the detective team, together with French Concession detectives, arrested the assassins, Li Decai and Guo Shanyu (both Anhui natives), and the accomplice, Guo Yushan. They were sent to the Second Special District Court, and the police lawyer filed a public prosecution against them for premeditated murder under Article 284 of the Criminal Code. The interrogation and confession details have already been reported in the previous issue. The case has been tried and concluded. Yesterday, the court handed down the sentence. The police escorted the three defendants to the court, where Judge Li Changnian presided over the First Criminal Court. He ordered Li and the others to be brought to the court and questioned briefly.

Li Decai and Guo Shanyu were sentenced to life imprisonment for conspiracy to murder, and deprived of civil rights for life. Guo Yushan was sentenced to 20 years of imprisonment for aiding and abetting murder, and deprived of civil rights for 20 years. The number of days Guo Yushan was detained before the trial would be counted as two days for one day of imprisonment. The murder weapon, a knife, was confiscated. After the sentences were pronounced, the three defendants were ordered to be detained in the prison pending further instructions during the appeal period.

Continued Notes on Maintaining Conditions for Used Clothing Employees 138

After the representatives of the Used Clothing Industry Workers' United Benefit Society petitioned the City Party Department the day before, according to the reports of the dismissed workers in each district, the number has been quite large.

However, layoffs usually occur after the autumn inventory, during the end of the sixth lunar month. Now, they have been advanced, which is obviously a retaliatory measure by the capitalists, making people embarrassed. With the goal of maintaining social peace and stability, a large number of representatives were sent to the Clothing Industry Association to petition in order to eliminate hidden dangers and avoid being despised by the outside world. (1) Request that the capitalists be urged to earnestly fulfill the conditions signed by both parties in 1927. (2) Layoffs should not be abused under the pretext of the autumn inventory. Letter 139

Editor: I have checked in the Shanghai section of your newspaper on August 7th (Citizens of Yinxiang District Oppose Latrine Bucket Donation). The so-called collecting of latrine bucket donations and extortion failed, driving away the old woman, etc., does not match the facts. The cleaning workers in this district have always been exploited and oppressed by the contractors in the Yinxiang District Cleaning Institute. Their monthly wages are less than 10 yuan. If they pass water, they must pay it to the government, without any money left. Therefore, most households have the practice of giving a small amount of alcohol money to show consideration and allow the workers to work with peace of mind. This alcohol money is given voluntarily by the residents and is not a forced collection of work. Later, this association discovered hooligans who were collecting money, so it prepared receipts and gave them to Ji Fu to give to the customers when receiving the alcohol money as proof and to prevent abuses. Therefore, the hooligans could not do it conveniently and were very resentful. They threatened workers in Tianfeng Lane to obstruct work and gathered an illegal so-called citizens' meeting, which was actually attended by their accomplices. There were fewer than 10 formal citizens. The so-called proposals were also packaged. The situation is like this. I am deeply afraid of confusing rumors. I hereby send this letter, hoping to make corrections. Sincerely, to the Shanghai Shenbao Newspaper, the Shanghai Seventh District Cleaning Industry Union.

Spring and Autumn

From "Construction" to A Renovation 142

— Chuan Ji Zhi

The progress of national construction is certainly attributed to Shanghai as a giant. Just speaking of houses,

From the former ghost weeping camps, desolate ruins rarely visited, now stand magnificent, towering, tall buildings and mansions; from the former narrow, rugged streets, now gradually opened up into flat asphalt roads, while the cramped, noisy shops on both sides are also demolished and renovated into new Western-style buildings. Shanghai's bright and splendid present is due to our gratitude to foreigners for opening up the concession, and to the unremitting efforts of the Chinese people to catch up. Recently, the huge waves of international economic panic spread from the other side of the Pacific to Shanghai's world trade market; at the same time, the collapse of the domestic rural economy also affected this ten-mile foreign market, resulting in an unprecedented commercial downturn, with every family "sacrificing greatly" and "great discounts" every day. Despite the continuous discovery of "opening great auspiciousness," business is enough to lead to wealth, so naturally some people muddle the waters to catch fish, and despite "opening great auspiciousness," they still shout "grand opening congratulations" with no increase. Rich people and landlords in the interior, due to the unstable situation, have also abandoned everything and come to the sea as leisurely absentee landlords, which has resulted in a situation of "more people than houses." Whether it is a shop or a house in a certain neighborhood, it is often reported as "full." In this way, smart entrepreneurs take the opportunity to invest in the construction business, so the east is renovated and the west is renovated, demolishing some of the older shops and houses and rebuilding them to suit the principle of "prosperous market." My friend Mr. S, seeing that Yangjingbang has been filled to become the current Avenue Edward VII, can of course be called "Old Shanghai." However, he left here last autumn and returned this summer. He no longer recognizes the Old West Gate, which shows Shanghai's rapid change.

However, the more houses that are renovated, the worse it is for poor friends, because they have no blessings to live in foreign houses for a lifetime. They watch the rich move in and are squeezed out of the urban living circle. Therefore, whether the progress of material civilization should be praised or cursed is really a difficult decision!

Results 144

— Xu Hongxia

Vertically, from ancient times to today, horizontally, from the South Pole to the North Pole, from the easternmost to the westernmost points, no matter how big or small the matter, there will always be "results."

Naturally, if a "cause" is sown, there must be a "fruit." Murder is the "cause," execution is the "result." Studying, becoming an official, becoming rich as an official, becoming wealthy, taking a concubine... these are all matters of mutual "cause" and "effect."

People say, "Nothing in the world cannot be done." "Done" means "result," "undone" means "no result." Therefore, there is absolutely nothing in the world that has "no result."

However, there is an exception outside the realm of theorems: China. In China, there are very few "fruits," and many tricks end with "no result" and then dissipate.

General assembly resolutions, three-year plans, five-year plans... these will not have "results." In short... Chinese people only have "causes" and will not have "results." Alas! China has very few "results," so in the future, it will inevitably reap a big "fruit."

Nanjing Road in Summer 145

— Ke Ding'an

At the end of spring this year, I don't know which astronomer, based on his observations, said, "There will be no summer this year." He even revealed it in the newspapers. At that time, two groups of people with different feelings of sorrow and joy expressed their opinions. Those with a pessimistic outlook were, of course, the general peddlers who relied on ice cream, plum juice, Dubinet soda, etc., and the big bosses of cold drink shops. They thought, "It must be fate. If the weather is not hot this year, how will we make up for the reduced income?" Those with an optimistic outlook were, of course, those who feared the heat like tigers. They thought, "It's a blessing from heaven that there's no summer this year. Not only can we greatly reduce summer spending, but we can also sweat less!" Who knew that facts are facts, and nothing can be forced. What is the current climate like? It is said that "for several days, it has been above 100 degrees." From this, it seems that the astronomer made the same mistake as Mr. Chan and Mr. Jia in misreading the next year's calendar. How laughable! The pavement of Nanjing Road is wider than other roads, so it can withstand more heat. The asphalt pavement, after being baked by the fierce sunlight, melts into a glue-like substance. Although the Public Works Department sprinkles fine sand on it, the rickshaw pullers who "earn their own living" still struggle desperately, running quickly. One day, I saw a rickshaw puller collapse on the road: many people watched, but no one could do anything!

Watering motorcars often shuttle back and forth on Nanjing Road. Although the main road surface temporarily receives some moisture, the friends in the shops along the roadside often smell a foul smell of water vapor. I don't know if this watering is hygienic or unsanitary. The followers of the Situ Temple (i.e., the Rainbow Temple) still fearlessly worship and prostrate themselves in the heat, lighting candles and burning incense. General incense candle shops still sell them in pairs of candles and one by one of incense to people.

"Summer Sales," "Special Sales," "Selling at Cost," "Bargain Sales," etc., of different banners, many can be seen on Nanjing Road. The buyers of the big companies, men and women, are still many. They don't seem to be afraid of the heat, and they still carry heavy things they bought in their hands.

The upscale cold drink shops, besides those opened by foreigners, also include many owned by Chinese. It is said that "their business exceeds previous years." The astronomer is a liar, actually "backfiring," so the big bosses laugh heartily. However, those who fear the heat suffer and complain to the heavens.

Northeast Fourth Company Commander 146

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 13: Abandoning Duty to Meet a Soulmate, a Beautiful Woman Silently Agrees; Inheriting the Family Business, a Strong Man Rejoices Wildly. After Zhao Ziqiang had that experience, he discovered that military life was, after all, tiresome. Moreover, after carefully calculating, it was extremely uneconomical. So, he went to the company headquarters, found Sergeant Wang Shili, and discussed this matter. Wang Shili was suddenly surprised to hear that the company commander wanted to resign. He looked at his face for a long time, unable to say a word. Zhao Ziqiang said seriously: It's true, I'm not going to do it anymore. It's not easy for a soldier to get out if he doesn't want to do it, but I'm a company commander who doesn't want to do it. There are plenty of people who want this position, so why would I be afraid of not being able to leave? Wang Shili said: Isn't that the end of it? There are many people who want to be company commander, so why throw away the existing company commander and not do it? You should discuss it privately with your close friends. Let's say a word in private: climbing from a soldier to a company commander takes a lot of effort. If you don't do it, the years of suffering you endured before will be somewhat inexplicable. If you knew that climbing to company commander was meaningless, you shouldn't have picked up a gun in the first place. These few words left Zhao Ziqiang unable to respond. After a long pause, he said: Coming to pick up a gun before was what I thought before. Not wanting to pick up a gun now is what I think now. Wang Shili was, after all, a person of lower status. Hearing him say this, he didn't dare to ask further, so he could only smile at him insincerely. When Zhao Ziqiang walked from his home to Yuanlai, he was thinking about his own reasons. He only thought that the money earned from the position of company commander was too insignificant, and it was not as good as picking buckets and selling vegetables, where he could still enjoy family happiness. What are people living for? Just to get up when the bugle sounds and eat when the bugle sounds? The more he thought about it, the more reasonable he felt, and there was not a single opposing thought to stop him. At this time, although Wang Shili said a few words lightly, but thinking carefully, his words also had reason. It is really not easy for a gun-carrying person to climb to be a company commander. Now that he resigns, wouldn't all previous efforts be in vain? (152)

World Rare News

About the Chicago World's Fair 147

— Huang Yingdai

The Chicago World's Fair, originally scheduled to open on June 1st, actually opened ahead of schedule on May 27th. After opening, because the scale of this World's Fair is so grand, it has created an unprecedented record. All the exhibits are sufficient to represent the progress of industry and commerce in the last hundred years. Therefore, everything is worthy of our attention. For this reason, I will report some trivial news:

The architecture of the Chicago World's Fair, because the scale is so grand, the architecture of the Chicago World's Fair is, of course, astonishing. The construction methods of all the exhibition halls are based on science. When the construction began, the planned construction cost was a total of US$11,000,000. However, the result exceeded this budget, and in addition to the construction undertaken by the General Assembly, some of the pavilions of various countries were built by themselves. The construction cost was at least 2,000,000 US$. In addition to the buildings, there are also public gardens and sports grounds. Architects from all over the world were gathered in one place to plan this Chicago World's Fair. The magnificence of the architecture can naturally represent an era in the history of architecture!

The security scale of the Chicago World's Fair is so grand. The value of the exhibits in the venue is inevitably incalculable, but we have already known from past experience that pickpockets and petty thieves are the most numerous at the World's Fair, so the loss of exhibits has also been heard from time to time. For this reason, this time at the Chicago World's Fair, great attention was paid to security. A lot of experienced and trained police officers and plainclothes detectives were recruited in advance to patrol back and forth and guard the various rooms. Some of the detectives had served in last year's Los Angeles Olympic World Games, so naturally they had outstanding detective skills and experience. In front of a famous French painting, there was even a special detective on duty to prevent theft.

Speaking of the detectives at the Chicago World's Fair, we must think of the thieves at the Chicago World's Fair. In general, the thieves in the United States, after hearing that the Chicago World's Fair was open, felt that this was an opportunity not to be missed, and they all came to Chicago to prepare to do a good business. Who knew that once they arrived in Chicago and entered the Chicago World's Fair, they found that the defense was so strict that the sharp eyes of the general detectives shot at them, and they were already frightened. Not to mention that there was no opportunity to steal the exhibits, they didn't even dare to pickpocket or dig pockets among the crowds of visitors, for fear of being arrested!

Transportation to the Chicago World's Fair Chicago was originally the center of American industry and commerce, so the railway is like a spider web. The important railways all take Chicago as the central station, so the transportation is also very convenient. During the opening period of the Chicago World's Fair, all the guests who came to visit could travel directly back and forth without any obstacles. However, the officials of the General Assembly, in order to facilitate the travel of visitors, also prepared a lot of public buses to drive directly to various places. In this way, the people of the United States, whether they live in the countryside or in the city, will find it very convenient.

The exhibits at the Chicago World's Fair This time, all countries exhibited their most beautiful products at the Chicago World's Fair and transported them for industrial and commercial competition. Among them, the United States' exhibits included the most cars and airplanes. The new cars and new airplanes from various factories were all displayed in one place, which was praised by the guests. As for China, it is the most pitiful, right? Because of the Sino-Japanese dispute, the government originally planned not to participate, but the people automatically transported the exhibits for display. There were very few industrial products among the exhibits, and the only thing that the Americans praised was China's silk weaving and embroidery. It is said that a Hunan embroidery was embroidered with a portrait of the American President Roosevelt. When the General Assembly closes, it will be presented to the American President Roosevelt. It is really pitiful to say that the rest of the exhibits cannot compete with the beauty of other countries!

Educational News

Special Feature on National Defense Education (2) 148

Professor Zhang Qiyun of Central University Lectures on Zi Tao's Notes: True national defense is not dead national defense, but living national defense. It does not teach people to die, but teaches people to live, that is, to achieve the least amount of danger and the greatest amount of comfort. Without the support of the entire nation, without the vision to use the strength of the entire nation to engage in war, only caring about teaching soldiers to go to the front line to fight and risk their lives, making them exposed to the yellow sand and making meaningless sacrifices, this is the most cruel and unkind thing in the world. National defense does not contain any mysterious meaning. As long as the people of the whole country do their best and work together towards the goal of national construction, they can achieve political integrity, everything is revitalized, and foreigners will have awe in their hearts invisibly, often making the enemy dare not even think of invading the Central Plains. This is the best policy for national defense. If we must wait for the enemy to attack before we start to resist, then it is impossible to prevent. If military fortresses are built in battlefield positions or border fronts for defense, it is still a medium policy for national defense. Looking at the natural hazards known as the first pass in the world, there is no artillery position and no military engineering with deep ditches and solid barriers. Isn't this the biggest joke?

Sun Tzu said, "If the defender is insufficient, the attacker has more than enough." The two words of national defense must not be interpreted incorrectly. What I hate to hear most is the recently popular term called "defensive national defense." How can there be reason to defend without being able to attack? After a place is lost, don't you want to counterattack? The reason why defensive national defense is inferior is that everything is passive rather than active, and everything is transferred according to the enemy's actions, like a shadow following a shape, and a yin pattern following a yang pattern, which is really a suffering to run for life. Taking the law from the middle can only get the lower. This is an inevitable trend. National defense, national defense, is not only for defense. Its defense is only for the preparation of opposition. Its opposition has the strongest power. Its power is enough to defeat the army of imperialists. Therefore, the ultimate goal of national defense is to win. How far is a passive strategy from non-resistance?

National defense has two aspects: intangible and tangible. The former is spirit, and the latter is material, but material comes with spirit, not spirit with material.

The year before last, Mr. Du Xigui went to Japan to investigate the navy and visited Marshal Togo Heihachiro of Japan at his private residence. He was a heavy and taciturn person. He said to Mr. Du, "If you come to our country to investigate the navy, you should pay attention to the spirit of the navy. Other things are not important." In addition to what he said, all were ceremonial words. Only to General Sa, the predecessor of our country's navy, did he inquire about his well-being. Mr. Du said, "Although I have repeatedly talked about the navy, the host seems unwilling to speak, and I am not convenient to ask again." With Togo's lofty position, his residence is no different from ordinary people, and his utensils are extremely simple, which is enough to be an example for our generation. He didn't want to say much about the navy. I don't know what his intentions were, but from his few words, I feel that a little is better than a lot.

I believe that the above four points are what the comrades who are currently advocating national defense education should pay attention to first and often observe.

Second Lecture on National Defense Education from an Educational Point of View 149

Everyone is a practical educator. There is no need for me to show off my knowledge of the general principles of education. For the sake of focusing attention, I still have to put forward a few points for discussion, and please give your advice.

㈠ National Accounting Theory in Education 150

Our knowledge theory is a tool to cope with the environment and overcome difficulties. The greatest difficulty is the difficulty of the country, that is, the so-called national crisis. Since China's education is a tool to transform China's environment and solve China's major problems, the education policy should focus on the entire national defense plan, and be a plan to prescribe the right medicine. The correctness and reliability of all teaching materials and methods also depend on whether they can have this function. If they can, they are real; if they cannot, they are false. Therefore, advocating national defense education should take the two words "function" as a prerequisite everywhere. For example, the function of submarines depends on the size of the country's naval power, and each has its own opinion. The United Kingdom has repeatedly advocated abolishing submarines, while France has fiercely opposed it. At the Washington Conference, the remarks made by the French plenipotentiary Mr. Briand were very interesting. When the United Kingdom, the United States, and Japan were arguing over the ratio of capital ships at 70% and 60%, Mr. Briand said, "France now does not discuss capital ships at all, but only wants submarines and cruisers." When the United Kingdom attacked France, he said to reporters, "The United Kingdom has Japan as an ally and is also friendly with the United States, but its capital ships have 500,000 tons of great navy. It is said that it is completely dealing with France, which it dare not do, or will it be used for large-scale deep-sea fishing? Therefore, France proposes to build a large number of submarines and will also engage in the study of underwater plants." What a pleasant and funny remark! When Mr. Du Xigui was investigating the navies of the major powers, Germany strongly urged China to build submarines, and Japan strongly argued that they were worthless. This is what Sima Zhao's heart is, and everyone knows it. Recently, the cry for aviation to save the country has been sung to the clouds, but the importance of submarines has not yet attracted attention. I remember that elementary school students in Hangzhou once raised money to build warships for the navy, but the education authorities said that it would be better to donate money for airplanes, which is quite disappointing. The function of submarines can make countries with weak naval strength not completely in a passive and defensive position, but can also engage in offensive actions. Submarines can not only be used within territorial waters, but also outside territorial waters. During the European War, German submarines once went to the coast of the United States and back, without having to replenish fuel. In naval warfare, submarines themselves do not have the power to determine the outcome, but they can also contain a part of the enemy's strength, so that the enemy's spirit is always at risk of being attacked. Moreover, the cost of building submarines is relatively low. The cost of building a battleship can at least build twenty or thirty medium-sized submarines. Therefore, most small and weak countries are working hard to equip themselves with submarines. According to our country's current national conditions, instead of expecting capital ships that cannot be obtained quickly, why not complete the construction of submarines first to meet the urgent needs of national defense? Mr. Huang Lizhou once said, "The way of learning is to be truly educated by what you can use yourself." The new theory of education also advocates "The way of education is to be truly educated by what can be used in your own country." The future of Chinese education must be adapted to national defense on the one hand, which is practical, not empty, and must be progressed in national crisis on the other hand, which is active, not static. Let us call it national accounting theory.

㈡ Theory of People's Livelihood in Education Education is life, and the school itself is a kind of life organization. The studies in the school must be quickly integrated with the life outside the school, so that every student can become a productive citizen. This is called the theory of people's livelihood in education. We do not advocate vocationalism. We believe that complete general education is far more valuable than narrow vocational training. Learning is to learn to be human. What is vocational education is nothing more than the knowledge and ability developed by general training, so that it can be active in a special position. However, in addition to work and occupation, there are other studies, especially the pure and supreme patriotism. Today, the strength of a country is not only based on the navy and army, but also on the national spirit of the country, that is, the so-called independent and unyielding spirit. We do not emphasize humanism either. We believe that the old-fashioned ideas, such as "laboring the mind" and "laboring the body," "governing people" and "being governed," should all be broken. Modern education is the education of the common people, which values both learning and thinking deeply and respects action and labor, adopting the principle of learning and doing at the same time, so that both production and training have a high speed. The above is an abstract theory. We can cite actual achievements to

prove it. During the Russo-Japanese War, the situation of Japanese agriculture greatly demonstrated its elasticity. The war had many effects on agricultural elements, such as hundreds of thousands of strong men throwing away their hoes and holding guns, and tens of thousands of horses leaving the fields and serving in the military. Even cattle were slaughtered for food. Agricultural labor was reduced so much by the war, and the increased burden on farmers due to the increased taxes and the raising of war debts was also very heavy, thus greatly reducing agricultural capital. However, Japanese farmers showed their sincere patriotism in this extraordinary period, economizing on food and clothing to make up for the lack of agricultural capital. Old, young, men, and women all worked together to make up for the lack of agricultural labor. Although the country had major events, the people were calm and heavy, and from the outside, they seemed unaware that there was a major war. For example, agricultural improvement, which was not easy to implement even with the most sincere encouragement in peacetime, was widely implemented during the war, and its results were also very significant. As a result, Japanese agricultural production presented an unprecedented harvest, such as the rice harvest being more than one-fifth higher than the average year, and wheat and silk also being superior to the average year's production. Japanese farmers are resilient and can work hard. The war lasted for two years, and they contributed brave soldiers, fine military horses, and abundant food to the country, and there was still more than enough. Undoubtedly, this is the effect of education in the twenty-odd years since the Meiji Restoration in Japan.

㈢ Theory of Age Order in Education

Education must be suitable for the students' level and psychological state. Mr. Graham Wallas, an Englishman who has studied political psychology, once said that "What is most likely to move children's emotions is not words, but scenery (Sight) and sound (Sonud). If you want children to love their country, you must lead them to see the scenery in their country or take them and put them in front of their eyes, such as great buildings, such as solemn ceremonies, which can deeply impress children's hearts and cannot be forgotten." Elementary school students' knowledge is just beginning to sprout, so they should first encourage their interest. Elementary school national defense teaching materials should focus on interesting stories and colorful models. The organization of the teaching materials only needs to be well thought out, and there is no need to solemnly announce it, because orderliness and system are not what children like. Junior high school students have gradually established a sense of order, and the general situation at home and abroad is gradually becoming clear. National defense teaching materials can be from simple to complex and from near to far, but in-depth theories are not yet the time. High school students can implement group methods according to different natures. Assuming that they are divided into three groups, namely the science group, the literature group, and the current affairs group, the national defense teaching materials must be selected separately and compromised to the most appropriate extent. Universities have more detailed majors, and the principle of teaching students according to their aptitude is more obvious. National defense education has direct and indirect relations with each department and field. Students can engage in in-depth research according to their interests and abilities. Generally, middle school students teach more than they learn, university students teach and learn equally, and in graduate school, there is no such thing as teaching, only focusing on research. Modern warfare is not only a war of soldiers, but also a war of science, or a martial arts competition of technology born from science. The weapons of war are not in the gunships and airplanes themselves, but in the industry that creates gunships and airplanes, or not in the industry of a country, but in the scientific research that creates the industry. Mr. Yan Jidao said, "If the people have a degree, then the ashes will be burned, and there will still be a day. Ignorant people will only harm things if they promote and encourage them."

㈣ Theory of Environment in Education

Education must not only teach according to the time and the students, but also teach according to the place. The operation of modern schools expresses its special color according to the local conditions, that is, the so-called local customs. For example, the education in Shanghai should pay more attention to maritime development and cultivate students' maritime thoughts and maritime spirit. If students cannot have a broad vision, this is an education that is out of touch with the times. There is a term in Europe that has not been seen in Chinese history, that is, maritime power, also known as sea power. In Japan during the Meiji period, all industries made great progress, and the most obvious was the shipping industry and the shipbuilding industry. The shipbuilding industry is a comprehensive industry. Almost all kinds of machinery industries in Japan are related to ships. The machinery industry of the shipyard not only contributes to the navy, but also to the air force and the army. The shipbuilding industry is developed, and the shipping industry is naturally developed, and maritime transport is the foundation of the navy. The rise and fall of maritime transport is the rise and fall of the country. When Japan has a national crisis, tens of thousands of seafarers can be quickly organized to meet the urgent needs. It can be seen that the success of the Japanese navy is not accidental. The 20th century is the era of the Pacific, a statement made by former US President Roosevelt. Roosevelt was the person who established the US naval policy and spared no effort to promote the navy throughout his life. In 1922, the government officially designated his birthday (October 27) as Navy Day. Recently, due to the dangerous situation in the Far East, Americans have paid more attention to this festival. Although China does not have a Navy Day, I hope that the education community in Shanghai will pay special attention to sea power and advocate for the coastal provinces. For example, the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau can find ways to contact the shipping industry to employ a few ships to train the shipping industry, which is specially used for students who are interested in maritime careers to learn navigation. Everything that should be known about maritime transport should be available, and the situation should be used to guide them, promote maritime interests, and cultivate navigation ideas as the prelude to the revitalization of the Chinese navy, because observation of everything in the world must precede the facts. There has never been a fact that can occur without an idea, which is also the meaning of what the Premier said that knowledge is difficult and action is easy.

Important News

Zhejiang Province Public and Private High School Graduates Exempted from Entrance Exams to Zhejiang University 151

In the past, during the University District era in Zhejiang Province, graduates of the Provincial Hangzhou High School with excellent grades were already entitled to exemption from entrance exams and guaranteed admission. Later, this was expanded to the Fourth, Seventh, and Tenth High Schools, as well as graduates of various provincial high schools. This year marks the first time that high school graduation qualification exams are being conducted. After consultation between the Department of Education and Zhejiang University, to encourage students with excellent results in the provincial high school qualification exams to further their studies, the previous method of guaranteeing admission without exams is temporarily revised. The number of guaranteed admissions for graduates of public and approved private senior high school general studies programs is expanded to fifteen. The qualification exam results will serve as the standard, with a score of 75 or higher and conduct grade B or higher at the original school considered qualified. As for the distribution of places, due to the larger number of graduates from provincial high schools, they are allowed six guaranteed admissions. The Fourth, Seventh, and Tenth High Schools will each continue to have two guaranteed admissions. The remaining three places will be awarded based on the individual performance of graduates from nine private high schools in the qualification exam who wish to attend Zhejiang University, selecting the best in order of merit, limited to a maximum of three. The Department of Education has issued a notice to all schools to submit their nominations before the 10th of this month, and to determine the departments to ensure compliance with the rule of no more than two students per department.

Educational Film Association Asks University Federation to Help Screen Educational Films 155

University students pay one yuan per semester and can watch a movie once every two weeks. The Shanghai branch of the Chinese Educational Film Association has already reported its plan to screen educational films in various schools next semester. The association sent a letter to the University Federation yesterday, requesting strong support when implementing the screening of educational films in various universities. The original letter is excerpted below: It is opened directly. In recent years, China's film industry has become increasingly developed. It is now imperative to use films to assist education and to follow the example of Europe and the United States. Last year, this association was initiated and organized by Mr. Wu Zhihui, Chu Minyi, Chen Lifu, Duan Xipeng, Guo Youshou, and others, and designated by the Ministry of Education as the representative organization for Chinese educational films, cooperating with international organizations. In order to implement film education as soon as possible, educational films are being collected from the International Educational Film Association of the League of Nations and various film companies at home and abroad, and this branch is entrusted to screen them in Shanghai first, taking Shanghai as an advanced city as a model for the whole country. Upon receiving the commission, this branch was established in accordance with the law and the implementation plan was formulated. Every two weeks, screenings will be held in schools at all levels. Each program will include not only interesting educational films, but also two or three reels of high-quality sound films or humorous newsreels, so as to make the audience more interested. All sound projectors and equipment will be provided by this branch. Schools without a large auditorium suitable for screening will rent a suitable venue for screening by this branch and invite students from nearby schools to visit. This method has long been effective in Europe and the United States. Young people's love of movies has become a universal phenomenon in modern times. Educational films are of great interest, and using them to cater to their preferences can naturally achieve the effect of imperceptible influence. However, this branch's expenses are limited, and the cost of going to various schools is very high, so it is necessary to slightly collect funds to supplement the expenses. The joint meeting of the first executive and supervisory committees decided to charge each student in colleges and universities one yuan per semester for educational film fees, which is recorded in the minutes. It is believed that the cost is minimal, but the benefits are substantial, and students from various schools should be willing to assist this great cause to benefit the country and society. However, educational film undertakings are still new in our country, and it is inevitable that some people will wait and see. It is hoped that your association, as the leading organization for university students, will sympathize and provide strong support. All schools will surely respond to the news. It is therefore earnestly requested that you send a letter to the authorities of various schools to strongly support this initiative, and notify the student unions of all schools to unanimously assist in order to facilitate the progress and achieve practical results. Sincerely,

Explanation of Qualifications for Selecting Students to Study in the UK by the Board of Trustees for the Management of the British Boxer Indemnity Fund 157

The Board of Trustees for the Management of the British Boxer Indemnity Fund is selecting students to study in the UK at public expense. Regarding academic fields such as shipbuilding, our country does not yet have specialized schools. Inquiries have been repeatedly received regarding how to stipulate the qualifications for candidates. The person in charge of the Board has now explained as follows: Shipbuilding (those who have studied mechanics may also apply), Aeronautical Engineering (those who have studied physics or mechanics may also apply), Geography (those who have studied history or geology may also apply), Geodesy (those who have studied astronomy, mathematics, physics, or civil engineering may also apply). Also, regarding specialized examinations, since our country's schools do not pay much attention to second foreign languages, the Board has been lenient in view of this. Candidates may choose one from the following subjects: Western History (French or German may be changed to Economics), Law (French or German may be changed to Constitution), Politics (French or German may be changed to International Public Law), Biology (French or German may be changed to Plant Geography), Shipbuilding (Ship Design may be changed to Mechanical Design). The deadline for registration has been extended by three days to August 18.
