Order of Pre-Selection for Next Year's Davis Cup 173

Netherlands, Italy, Austria, and Germany have the advantage

Since the International Tennis Federation decided on the new game

After the competition system, it has been implemented this year. Although France once proposed to cancel it, it still failed to pass with a vote of six to seven. According to the content of the new system, the four countries that have the right to the European Zone semi-finals this year and the countries that have the right to the re-election of the countries that win the re-election competition in other countries can participate in the competition next year. The re-election competition will start this year. Therefore, those who do not participate in the competition this year must wait until next year to participate. The Davis Cup competition next year has actually started this year. The order of the re-election competition this year is recorded as follows:

Belgium, Hungary, Belgium, Sweden, Netherlands. 1. Romania, Poland, Poland, Italy, Italy, Monaco, Switzerland. 2. Norway, Yugoslavia, Austria, Spain, Austria. 3. Denmark, Greece, Germany, Ireland, Denmark, Germany. 4. Each week's date. The first week, Belgium vs. Hungary, ended on July 23. The second week is scheduled to end before August 20. The third week ends on September 3. There are still four groups that have not competed in the second week.

The competition situation. Among the four groups, the Netherlands has a good chance of winning in the first group, Italy has no problem in the second group, Austria in the third group, and Germany in the fourth group. The overall situation is like this. The countries that have the right to the semi-finals this year are England, Australia, Japan, and the Czech Republic. These eight countries will compete next year. England won the Davis Cup this year and will be replaced by France. There are not many participating countries in the Americas, so this system has not been implemented.

The American women won the Anglo-American international tennis tournament and the Wiedemann Cup for the seventh year in a row.

Page 15

Free Talk

The Discount on Grandiose Words 178

— Wei Suo

The discount on grandiose words is, in fact, a discount on literature. An author's self-description often needs to be discounted. Even admitting to being pitiful and useless is not a "fixed price," let alone grandiose words.

The talented Li Bai's fondness for grandiose language goes without saying. Even the gaunt and skeletal literary genius Li Changji, who grew long fingernails, said, "I'll buy a sword from the Ruoye Creek, and tomorrow I'll return to serve Lord Yuan," which was utterly unrealistic; he wanted to be an assassin. This should be discounted to zero. The proof is that he never actually did it. During the difficult times of the Southern Song Dynasty, Lu You was naturally one of the passionate patriots. He once said, "I am still capable of crossing the vast desert; why do you all weep at the New Pavilion?" He was actually unable to go and this should also be discounted to zero. However, I don't have the book at hand, and there might be errors in the quoted poem, so I'll preemptively apply a discount here.

In fact, this habit of feigning grandiose words is not unique to men of letters. Common people or merchants also engage in it frequently. When individuals A and B fight in the market, the loser usually says, "I recognize you!" This means that they will be like Wu Zixu, vowing revenge. However, most of the time, they never actually do it. If they are intellectuals, they might resort to some conspiracy. But for common people, this is often the end of the struggle. The words are spoken without sincerity, and the listeners don't take them seriously. Over time, it has become a kind of ritual to end a fight.

Old novelists have long seen through this situation. When writing about prostitutes arguing with each other, they typically attack the other person for having an affair and then declare, "I am someone who can stand on my fingertips and have people stand on them, someone on whose arms horses can run..." What happens next? They let others apply their own discount. They know that others will never be so foolish as to believe them completely, but they still have to say it, just like quack doctors who print "Intending to deceive the world, struck by thunder and burned" on their packaging - it becomes a kind of ritual.

But due to different circumstances, some people immediately apply their own discounts. For example, in advertisements, we sometimes see people claiming, "I am someone who sits without changing my name and walks without changing my surname." This genuinely evokes a sense of respect, as if one were encountering a character from "The Seven Heroes and Five Gallants." But then it continues with, "Even if I sometimes use other pen names, I am responsible for all the articles I publish." Then they twist their body and disappear like Tu Xingsun. Do I like to "use other pen names"? I have no choice. Shanghai is originally a part of China and naturally receives Confucius's teachings. Even merchants have "fixed price" signs inside their shops that constantly reflect the "big sale" banners outside, but they always have a green reason: either promoting national goods or commemorating the opening.

Therefore, self-discounting is still not enough. Any "old Shanghai" resident must apply another discount.

Conjecture 179

— Xu Maoyong

Today's students generally think about career paths before even applying to schools, often anxiously looking at a large newspaper full of enrollment advertisements. Liberal arts are absolutely out of the question. Hasn't the Ministry of Education already been restricting the enrollment of liberal arts students? If China's industry could develop, then it would be best to enter engineering, but that "development" is not necessarily guaranteed. Should one enter law school to become a judge or a lawyer? Should one enter business school to become a banker? Studying radio or aviation is the most fashionable, or perhaps one should enter a foreign language school and then work for foreigners in the future. Otherwise, one could become a translator. To be quick, study Japanese...

For female students, sericulture, kindergarten teaching, and obstetrics were previously reliable options, but now they are all somewhat unreliable. Recently, several provinces are planning to establish female police forces. Therefore, "becoming a police officer" has become a new and stable path in their minds.

This kind of thinking was called "conjecture" by Wang Chong of the Han Dynasty, which is similar to what is now called "speculation." However, it has even less certainty than commercial speculation.

Wang Chong's "Lunheng" records a failed "conjecturer," "weeping on the road, lamenting his old age and lost opportunities." When asked why he couldn't succeed, he said:

"When I was young, I studied literature. When my literary talents were accomplished, I wanted to become an official, but the ruler liked to use old men. When the old ruler died, the next ruler used military men. I changed to the military. When my military skills were accomplished, the military ruler also died. When the young ruler came to power, he liked to use young men, and I was already old. That is why I have never had an opportunity!"

The world is too complex, and changes happen too quickly. The certainty of successful "conjecture" has truly become "a sliver." Therefore, the result can only be random "chance," like using ten copper coins to try for a lottery prize of five hundred thousand.

However, I have "conjectured" a path that is foolproof, and now I am willing to offer it to confused young people. This path is: learn to fight.

China's civil wars will probably last for many years, requiring soldiers. External wars will eventually happen, requiring national heroes. If a revolution comes, it will need soldiers. If all else fails, and one needs to "go to Liangshan," one must be a hero. Someone who knows how to fight has many career paths.

In rural temples, recruitment banners are displayed year-round. Military academies, central military and political schools, etc., also recruit students every year. There are many career paths.

Talking About "The Ballad of Zhaojun" 180

— He Ru

I once read a poem by Wang Jian of the Tang Dynasty, "Watching a Southern Barbarian Prostitute," which said, "Wanting to tell the story of Zhaojun, she gathers her emerald eyebrows, her clear voice winding and lamenting in song. Which young man in the spring breeze throws her gold coins and asks her to sing more?" This barbarian prostitute made a living by singing and telling the story of Zhaojun. It is unknown what form her performance took - Suzhou ballads? Drum ballads? Or flower drum folk songs? Furthermore, the Complete Tang Poems contains a poem by Ji Shilao, a poet whose lineage and official rank are untraceable, entitled "Watching a Shu Woman Perform The Ballad of Zhaojun," which says, "The enchanting woman has not yet donned her pomegranate skirt, but claims her family is connected to the Jinshui River. Her coral lips know the events of a thousand years, and her clear words are worthy of lament in the autumn wind. The crescent moon on the border is reflected in her furrowed emerald brows, and the clouds beyond the Great Wall are depicted when the painting scroll opens. She tells of all the sorrows of silks and satins in those days, conveying Zhaojun's feelings to Wenjun." This Shu woman sang and told the story of Zhaojun, and even displayed a painting scroll of Zhaojun departing for the frontier. The title of the poem, "perform," is obviously an abbreviated term for "performing and reciting," which has been used since the Six Dynasties for monks chanting Buddhist scriptures. The term "ballad" should be the meaning of Bianwen. Thirty years ago, handwritten copies from the Li Tang and Five Dynasties periods were discovered in the Dunhuang Stone Chamber in Gansu, including The Great Maudgalyayana Saving His Mother from Hell Bianwen, Shun the Filial Son Bianwen, The Demon Subduing Bianwen, The Jataka Tales Bianwen, etc., totaling thirty or forty types. This literary form mixes prose and verse, with both speaking and singing, seemingly with singing as the center. Recently, I saw Liu Fu's Dunhuang Gleanings, which includes a type tentatively titled Zhaojun's Departure, although the original title is unknown. The text contains many fragments and errors. I will now quote a section describing Zhaojun's death to provide a glimpse.

Since last night, Mingfei has gradually weakened. Because of foreign things, she will mostly not survive. The Xiongnu chief solemnly sacrifices to the mountains and rivers, repeatedly praying to the sun and moon. He seeks methods in every possible way, requesting techniques a thousand times. ...... Just at the third watch, her life came to an end. The Xiongnu chief took off his emperor's clothes and put on the clothing of a commoner. With disheveled hair, he mourned the deceased. The tribal leaders all arrived. Brave warriors did not leave the side of the deceased, and the tribes dared not go east or west. They wailed day and night, unable to stop even for a moment, with sorrowful and poignant tones. How can one describe the place where Mingfei cried!

Zhaojun died at midnight last night, and the Turks sent messengers in haste this morning. Messengers gallop on horseback along the three borders, conveying the Xiongnu chief's orders, while a non-written message is sent ten thousand miles to the Han Emperor. The Xiongnu chief personally attended the mourning on this day, unwilling to leave even for a moment to watch over the deceased. He unsheathed his sword and removed his emperor's hat, letting his hair down and putting on the clothing of a commoner. ...... The cold wind entered the tent, and the sound was still bitter. The dawn sun approached, but the crying had not yet stopped. The nights of sleeping together in the past were so short, but now sleeping alone feels like forever. Who would have thought that she would be so far away from the capital, never again remembering lying in the dark land of the north? If I had known that death would mean burial in the sand, I would have regretted not letting you return to the imperial homeland. This literary form is just like Bianwen. Could this be the Ballad of Zhaojun sung and told by the barbarian prostitute and the Shu woman? Luo Zhenyu's naming it The Biography of Mingfei is certainly not correct, and Hu Shi's naming it The Song of Mingfei is also incorrect. Liu Fu's tentative title of Zhaojun's Departure is still not appropriate. Four years ago, I wrote The Ballad of Zhaojun, which was published in the Nanguo Weekly. I first named it The Ballad of Zhaojun, but it received little attention. Recently, I saw Zheng Zhenduo's Illustrated History of Chinese Literature, which called this text Mingfei Bianwen. I don't know if he saw my article first? I still firmly believe that the name The Ballad of Zhaojun is more justified, and I ask Mr. Hu (Shi), who has a penchant for textual research and history, to agree with my statement.

Javanese Summer 181

— Huang Renjie

Whenever summer arrives and I feel unbearably hot, I often recall my second hometown, Java, which I left many years ago.

Java has no so-called summer. The climate there is almost the same all year round. People who have never been to Southeast Asia always think that the climate in tropical areas must be very unbearable, but it is not actually the case. For example, in Java, the hottest time of day is only two or three hours, and the rest of the time it is very cool. Sometimes you even have to cover yourself with a blanket at night.

In Shanghai, apart from the very few wealthy people who can escape to distant places like Lushan and Moganshan to avoid the summer heat, it is impossible for the rest of the middle class or those who live on salaries to find a cool place near Shanghai to escape the scorching heat for a few hours. The suburbs of Shanghai are unbearable, full of filth, coffins, and tombs, without a single hill or forest.

But it is not like that in the cities of Southeast Asia. While the wealthy merchants have their own places to spend money, the middle class and those who live on salaries also have their own places to escape the summer heat.

Speaking of which, one cannot help but thank the Westerners who are always eager to claim that they are civilizing foreign races. Now, the major cities of Java, such as Batavia, have architecture that is so well-organized and streets that are so clean that they are comparable to any city in Europe, not to mention the suburbs outside the cities, which have all been cleaned and beautified by them to an extraordinary degree.

When I lived in Batavia, I often invited two friends to take a motorcycle to the suburbs for a cool breeze in the afternoon when the sun was setting. The motorcycle sped along the wide asphalt road lined with coconut trees, and the cool breeze brushed our faces, dispelling all the summer heat. Looking at the roadside, there were lush green rice fields, shady orchards, dense rubber trees, and neat sugarcane fields, a beautiful scene created by the combination of nature and human effort, truly enough to please the eye and gladden the heart.

Afterwards, we would choose a quiet place to park the motorcycle, either in the open space in front of a native hut or on the deserted ridges of a field. We would spread out the cool mats we had brought, and then one by one, we would take out the phonograph, soda, beer, snacks, etc. from the car. We would sit down and eat, play, and chat. After eating, we would lie down and breathe in the fresh air of the countryside, inhaling the fragrance of plants and trees that could not be breathed in the city, and listening to the singing of insects and birds that could not be heard in the city. Everyone felt that their worldly worries had been completely discarded and unconsciously entered a dreamy world of fairyland. It was not until a crescent moon hung high in the sky that we sat up, packed up our things, and drove back on the clean and cool road.

Is such pleasure something that can be enjoyed in the great Eastern metropolis of Shanghai? The past is like smoke, and when I think back on it, I can only yearn for it.

Ordinary Matters (34) 182

— Dan Guosun

"For this matter, let me have Suiwu take care of it! It's easy to handle, easy to do." Then Yongsun called Suiwu over, explained the situation to him, and told him to hurry up and take care of it. Later, he added, "Go find Eulenspiegel first, Suiwu; if you can't negotiate well, then find Romanes and Icarus. Among these three people,"

"There will always be someone who has a solution."

"Okay, Uncle," Suiwu said. "So, from which day do we start?" "Start from New Year's Eve."

"I'll go take care of it tomorrow; you'll get a response immediately." Yongsun, of course, was used to this kind of method, but Lao Wu was truly grateful. As for Zichun, although she initially had some discomforting doubts amidst her pleasure, she later thought that it wouldn't hurt to do this kind of cost-free business a few times in secret, so she treated it with magnanimity. So, this man and woman just stared expectantly, waiting for Suiwu's reply. Little did they know that before two or three o'clock, the patriotic heroes of Zhabei had already begun to implement resistance against the enemy!

This glorious and unprecedented change, which occurred right under the noses of the imperialists, naturally diminished our faith in their paper-tiger-like traditional beliefs. And they also obviously reduced their faith in themselves, so they temporarily blocked all places like the "No. 281" that they had always allowed to be secretly open using the method of covering one's ears while stealing a bell. At the same time, those customers also felt that their material supplies were not as abundant as before, so in the first five or six days, no one had the mind to think about that kind of amusement. We don't need to say that Zichun and Lao Wu had both given up. But after a week, the public's fear of war seemed to have gradually subsided, and since it was just the Lunar New Year, everyone felt a bit itchy, so some people secretly gathered a few like-minded companions and started doing it on a small scale. Someone like our Yongsun, who had a wide range of acquaintances and a strong interest in pleasure, was naturally one of these people. He did it for two or three days and felt dissatisfied, and everyone else also felt dissatisfied. So he thought of Lao Wu again, and then he planned how to fulfill that promise he had made to Lao Wu before.

In fact, his plan was realized in less than three days. The ones who provided the houses for the hideouts were those foreigners wearing tiger skins, like the "Dues" and the "Ness." The ones who provided the capital to be the house were several wealthy friends of Yongsun. The ones who provided the effort to host and split the profits were Lao Wu's "family." In addition, there were people like Suiwu who advertised, handled things, and took care of things outside. These people, who abandoned everything and thought that they could secretly enjoy themselves in a timely manner, amused themselves in the east today and in the west tomorrow. They were really energetic. But little did they know that the police were already regarding them as a flock of fat sheep, just waiting for a way to subdue the shepherd wearing the tiger skin and then catch them all in one fell swoop!

That night, of course, he also happily spent his time at this venue.

Business Sutra 27 198

Banks of the Huangpu River... Paths of Sichuan

The High and Low Prices of Jellyfish Are Mutually Different by Zheng Xintian 199

丨A Commoner's Dish in Shanghai… A Delicacy on the Table in Sichuan丨Jellyfish is a unique marine product of our country. The scientific name is medusa, also known as Shimu, belonging to coelenterate animals. It is shaped like an open fabric, semi-smooth and soft. The color is light blue, and the thin skin is commonly known as "jellyfish skin." Below are eight arms, extending like handles, with a light red color, commonly known as "jellyfish head."

Jellyfish is mainly produced in Daishan, Huanglong, and Sijiao and other small islands in Dinghai, Zhejiang. Every year in May, as the mold spreads, these types of jellyfish appear in the nearby seas, floating on the surface. Fishermen catch them and place them in large barrels. They are soaked in salt and alum for about three or four times. The water gradually decreases, and the color also turns slightly yellow. Then they are taken out and stacked in bamboo fences, covered with mesh-shaped bamboo filaments. Each piece is about two and a half feet high and weighs about 300 jin. After being packed, they are transported to Shanghai and sold to salted fish shops or seafood shops.

To distinguish the quality of jellyfish, the "Chen" character in the common saying "Chen jellyfish" is sufficient to describe it. "Old is precious." Jellyfish skin must have 1) a bright yellow color, 2) large round sheets, and 3) a dry and thin texture. Those that meet these criteria are considered good. Jellyfish heads are similar, but the color should be white and tender. Red ones are fresh and not crisp when eaten. Jellyfish is produced in the near sea, so the selling price is extremely cheap. Jellyfish skin is about 11 or 12 yuan per dan, while jellyfish head is only about 6 yuan. In small vegetable markets, one or two hundred wen can buy a large sheet. People appreciate its cheapness and because it is easy to wash and has a crisp and delicious taste, everyone likes to eat it. The proverb "jellyfish radish shreds..." is used because it is cool and refreshing, has a unique flavor, and is deeply in line with the common people's taste.

In addition to being sold in this port, the largest sales outside the port are from the Guangdong and Sichuan dealer groups. People in those areas regard jellyfish as a treasure, especially in Sichuan. The further away from the sea, the more difficult it is to obtain, and the more frequent the transportation along the way. The cost is high, and it cannot be sold for less than five or six jiao per jin in Sichuan. Sichuan gentry use it when entertaining guests, while common people feel a sense of inhibition, which is close to being aristocratic. It is the same thing, but the high and low prices are mutually different in different places. Things are valued when they are rare. This is true of jellyfish, and it is true of everything. The essence of things has no inherent value.

Commentary

Entered the Zoo 200

— Jie Xin

Every time the wind is cold or the heat is oppressive, I realize that another semester is coming to an end. These past two days, I rushed to hand in the students' exam papers to the academic affairs office, so I felt extraordinarily relaxed and refreshed, as if I had cleared a heavy burden! At the same time, this also means that my life as an elementary school teacher has passed another semester. But what have I gained in a semester?! The factual answer is truly heartbreaking! It seems that this has become a common phenomenon. Many people always ridicule and despise elementary school teachers. They seem to think that elementary school teachers are insignificant. The reason for this is that the current elementary school teachers are too complex. There are all kinds of people. Almost anyone who has nothing to do and can hum a few sentences has stepped onto this teaching platform. Therefore, the status of elementary school teachers has invisibly declined. However, the entire glory of being an elementary school teacher is completely bankrupt because of this. Is this people's arrogance or the cruelty of the times? ...

This time, I went to do this thing voluntarily. I mustered up the courage and spirit to take the risk. I was not subjected to any pressure or driven by life or dominated by the environment, and no one encouraged me. I wanted to adjust my life. I needed to be close to the innocence of children, because only in innocence can I find the truth. But half a year of experience tells me that I can't help but feel infinite sadness! In the past ten years, I have been detained in dark and sunless church schools. Although I had previously attended co-educational schools, it was only in that one year when I was very young. So when I first came to this school with male and female colleagues and classmates, I couldn't help but feel another kind of situation and feel unnatural, especially since it was my first time working. But after thinking it through, I blamed myself for being too pedantic and too shallow! Since I have embarked on the journey of society, if I need true equality between men and women, then why do I have these unnecessary scruples? So I boldly started talking to them. In fact, talking is just this one thing. But one thing that made me strange was that colleagues usually wear different masks and suspect each other. Is this probably the so-called art of dealing with the world? I was originally very childish, always speaking frankly and casually. Later, I gradually realized that I was too naive, so I pretended to be mature. So I joined a huge dye vat, drifting away my inherent innocence, stained with the art of dealing with the world. As for the mask, of course, it was unconditionally added! However, this kind of behavior is so against my conscience!

The age of elementary school students is too uneven. The students in the senior classes are quite old. Some are even older than me, and some are taller than me. But when they come to the office to talk to me, they first take off their hats and salute and reveal their innocent naivety. Only this is enough to make me feel an unspeakable emotion and situation! Ah, but where do I start? Because their actions are all fake! The disappointment and trauma this gave me are so profound! I have deeply entered the zoo, and all around me are hideous and terrifying!

Even so, I have never compromised. I want to avoid the past - this cursed past, and I am not afraid to look forward to the future - this illusory and elusive future. I should fight with my strength to create, to create the present - a bright present!

Mr. Ma Henian's Painting (Brief Biography) 201

I am a Confucian scholar who also loves calligraphy and painting. After giving up the imperial examination, I taught for twenty years. In my old age, I was unable to do so, so I came to Shanghai to paint landscapes. I had no entry to formal training in the area where heroes gather. I dare not show off my small skills. Driven by the environment, I had to follow Mao Sui's self-recommendation. I hope that the great masters will not laugh at me. Ma Henian.

Mrs. Zhang's Kitten 202

— Yi Ping

The little tabby cat that had been missing for three days was meowing at my feet again during lunch. It looked even more haggard, thin, and pitifully gazed up at me like a dying beggar. I couldn't help but think of the little tabby cat's owner, Mrs. Zhang.

Mrs. Zhang was a kind old woman around fifty years old. Three years ago, she rented a small room in my house and lived alone. She had no relatives coming and going, and she never stepped out of the door. She also didn't like to talk, like other older women who liked to nag about the affairs of the west family and the gossip of the east family. After living here for a long time, she didn't have much contact with the neighbors. Occasionally, when she met them at the door, she would say a few words about the weather today and whether they had eaten, and then bow her head to caress the little tabby cat in her arms. It was her only companion and only way to pass the long years. Mrs. Zhang mixed with it like a child, sometimes murmuring to it, seeming to tell the little tabby cat her pitiful life story. But what did the little tabby cat know? It only meowed, but in Mrs. Zhang's ears, the little tabby cat's meows were an expression of sympathy for her. The little tabby cat was indeed very cute, with a small body, a pair of emerald green eyes shining on both sides of its black nose, two yellow circles on its back, like two Bagua diagrams on a Taoist's python robe, and its whole body was snow-white. When it chased butterflies in the green grass, it looked like a rabbit.

Time urged people to age, and Mrs. Zhang had lived in our small room for a year. She was still as silent and lonely as when she first came. Other than eating, drinking, and sleeping, she played with her little tabby cat, or she had a few more strands of white hair.

That autumn, I got married, and relatives and neighbors all sent gifts to congratulate me. When they saw my mother, they shouted "Congratulations" and "Blessings," which aroused Mrs. Zhang's sorrow. She thought that doing happy events would bring good luck, so she went back to her small room alone and cried loudly. Finally, a neighbor woman found out her life story.

Her family was also of middle-class origin. Her husband ran a southern goods store in the city with his own funds, and their life was of course well-off. However, after they got married, they had no children. They sought signs and divinations all year round, built bridges and paved roads. It was not until she was in her thirties that she got her wish and gave birth to a son. Needless to say, the couple loved him like a treasure. Later, after the father died, the child was spoiled and stole money from home to gamble and visit prostitutes. The southern goods store lost too much money and finally closed down. He stole Mrs. Zhang's clothes and jewelry and never returned.

Mrs. Zhang cried and said, my son is here, and he is as big as the young master of the landlord. When I see other people's sons getting married, I think of my own son, and I can't help but cry.

After this secret was revealed, the neighbors all felt sorry for Mrs. Zhang and were very close to her because of her taciturn and silent smile.

Last year was also a summer with cicadas chirping. Four soldiers came to our street, saying that they were ordered by the officer in charge to pick up Mrs. Zhang. The villagers couldn't bear to see people carrying guns and secretly discussed it, thinking that Mrs. Zhang might be some kind of secret figure. I asked clearly the surname of their officer, which was exactly Mrs. Zhang's son. Mrs. Zhang was so happy at that time that she just recited Buddha in the sky, packed a little valuables, and left with the four soldiers. She said that she would ask her son to come and thank the landlord and all the neighbors in a few days. Now it is summer again with cicadas chirping. We have not known her whereabouts since then, but the cute little tabby cat left behind has not seen its owner and does not think about eating and drinking all day long, meowing and rolling at my feet, seeming to ask me where its owner has gone. Looking at its more haggard and thin body, I can't help but think of Mrs. Zhang.

Humorous Prose

Gandhi of India Opens 203

— Luo Fei

In India recently there lived a great man. His name Gandhi is known throughout the globe. He knew the pain of a fallen people. Nonviolent resistance to strong England. His actions are strange and eccentric. He often goes around naked. He was arrested several times without fear. He often fasts with a firm determination. This ambition is admirable. He won't stop until his goal is achieved. He is willing to sacrifice his life. He only wishes the Indian people to be self-governed. The authorities are therefore jealous of him. They arbitrarily arrest him and imprison him. The news from the former dynasty came quickly. It said that Gandhi had been imprisoned again. He abandoned the monastery he had practiced in that year. He encouraged his comrades with moving words. The case concerns politics, no small matter. The judgment must be two years. British planes demonstrated their power. They flew over the whole village of Kotkai. All the villagers fled. There was not a single person in the village. Gandhi was originally an important person.

The Ever-Elusive Bedbug 204

— Yu Zhang

Shanghai has many bedbugs; this is no exaggeration. Their traces can be found in almost everything you use, wear, and eat. For example, in the bed you sleep on, the stool you sit on, the clothes you wear, even in the food you eat. I once saw bedbugs on the shiny, oiled paper wrapping bread! This is the most remarkable news I have encountered in my life. However, it's only because I'm new to Shanghai. Old Shanghai hands are used to it and wouldn't make a fuss.

Recently, because I've been preparing for school entrance exams, I've been studying and thinking hard every day, not daring to rest for a moment. From eight o'clock in the morning to twelve, and from one o'clock to five in the afternoon, I'm using my brain for almost ten hours a day. By evening, I'm extremely tired. The weather is also so hot, and because I don't like sweating, I can't go to sleep early. So, I always have to wait until nine o'clock before I can sleep soundly. This, of course, is the happiest and sweetest time of my day. Needless to say, I fall asleep the moment I touch the pillow. But who knew that less than twenty minutes into my peaceful sleep, those hateful bedbugs would come to invade me, preventing me from sleeping soundly, waking me from my sweet dreams? When I touched my body, I felt many tiny, raised, flesh-colored bumps. These raised areas looked red and swollen and felt itchy and painful. At first, I was still drowsy and just scratched a few times before falling back asleep. But who knew the second invasion would again prevent me from sleeping? I had no choice but to get up, turn on the light, and go back to the bed to catch them. I searched almost all around the bed, but I couldn't see a single bedbug. I was really puzzled at this point. I clearly knew that bedbugs were harassing me, but how come I couldn't see them? Being sleepy, I had to go back to sleep drowsily, too lazy to investigate the matter further. But in an instant, I was disturbed in the same way again! I tried again, and when I turned on the light, the invaders had again escaped to the ninth heaven. I hated it! I was amazed! How could such tiny creatures have such nimble senses and clever instincts? Can't humans compete and win against them? At that moment, I was already extremely tired, and the god of sleep was relentlessly surrounding me. I had no choice but to go back to sleep. But after the fourth disturbance, I came up with a plan. I woke up the person in the same room as me and asked her to turn on the light for me. Haha! As expected, human intelligence eventually prevailed. At that moment, I found many small, red bedbugs crawling all over me, looking smug. But could they still escape? In less than five minutes, I had caught them all. Only then could I sleep peacefully until the next day.

And what about the next day? I really can't continue to imagine! The next night, weren't they still active? And there were even more of them, and their fighting power was even fiercer. I was already at my wit's end. But in this helplessness, I understood! "They are entirely for the sake of survival!"

Under the Traffic Lights (47) 205

— Xi Lin

(25) It's alright if your hair is curly, as long as your heart is upright. '...General XX graduated from the Japanese Military Academy and has held important military positions in the Northeast. Since Zhang Xueliang surrendered the three provinces without resistance, General XX was filled with righteous indignation and automatically commanded his troops to resist the enemy on the XX border. Recently, due to running out of ammunition and supplies, he has come to Shanghai to personally represent the army, hoping that patriotic people from all walks of life will generously donate to him, so that the recovery of lost territory can be hoped for. Now, please welcome General XX to give a speech and report on the situation on the battlefield.' As usual, there was a round of applause. General XX wore a worn-out Zhongshan suit, showing his identity as a veteran of many battles. However, his curly hair and delicate hands were out of keeping with his appearance. But who would pay attention to these details? Moreover, our General had already stood up, and there was another round of applause as usual. The situation at the front that he reported was roughly the same as that reported by the previous representatives who came to Shanghai, so it doesn't need to be described in detail. However, he had a special insight that was admired by the audience. He said:

'…Although we have gone through so many battles, we absolutely do not want to boast and brag in order to win the beautiful name of national hero. Maybe the Chinese people know very little about our army. We only hope to die for the sake of saving the country, and die without a heroic name.'

Therefore, Hu Yuanliang immediately proposed that the XX Association should allocate a donation of X thousands to be taken to the front by General XX. Even those who opposed it were too embarrassed to raise their objections, so the proposal was passed without dissent.

After the meeting, Wang Huaxi accompanied General XX back to the residence. This Wang residence was naturally no longer the small attic room of the past. The living room was decorated quite luxuriously. Mrs. Wang had already excused herself and gone upstairs. Here, Wang Hua closed the door of the front hall and, half-walking, half-jumping, pulled General XX to sit down beside him. He wanted to say something triumphant at first, but later he felt that the matter was not over and that there was still a need to pay attention to it, so he said:

'Yi Ping, what we need to pay attention to now is your feelings for the XX News Agency in the North. Although you fooled everyone today with your words about wanting to be an unknown hero, now that you are famous, you need the XX News Agency to constantly fabricate news from the front to publish in the newspapers. If you are exposed, it won't be a laughing matter. How about sending a telegram tonight?'

The General pondered for a long time and replied in a sophisticated manner:

'Old Wang, you have been in the game for nothing your whole life. Since I'm somewhat confident, if XX doesn't want to fabricate news for us, it's okay, since we've already agreed on several tens of thousands, we can just send them more money. Even if they really refuse, we might as well mobilize the Japanese radio station in Qinhuangdao, because recently the strategy of the Japanese military is to create false numbers and false victory news about the Northeast Volunteer Army in China in order to calmly prepare their strength in our false display of power and eliminate the Volunteer Army, while the country is deceived by the victorious situation and does not make further preparations. Therefore, their radio station in Qinhuangdao specializes in catching shadows and spreading all kinds of news about the Volunteer Army. It's a pity that the news received by Chinese news agencies is mostly broadcast by Qinhuangdao. In this case, even if the XX News Agency understands our inside story and doesn't publish it, they can't prevent other news agencies from doing so!'

The clever General began to unbutton his Zhongshan suit, revealing a snow-white shirt inside. A scent of perfume mixed with body heat wafted out, but there was no sweaty smell of a soldier. Wang Hua became excited and said with a flourish:

'Wonderful, wonderful! Then, I'll quickly ask Yuanliang to write a news report saying that you will be setting off tomorrow to the front. Actually, you have to personally go to Qinhuangdao. I think you should take five thousand first, and then I'll send the rest.'

As Wang Hua stood up to go out, the General had already taken off his Zhongshan suit, put on his own handsome Western-style suit, and went to the mirror to tie his tie. He suddenly noticed his curly hair and wondered if it had given him away at today's meeting, but he immediately smiled and joked:

"It's alright if your hair is curly, as long as your heart is upright!"

Movie Special

Fairbanks and Pickford Agree to Divorce 206

— Lonely Palm

I remember five or six years ago when the movie martial arts star Douglas Fairbanks and his wife, "America's Sweetheart" Mary Pickford, came to Shanghai, they caused a sensation among movie fans. Last year, Fairbanks came to Shanghai again, but he was alone. Mary Pickford was in Hollywood, guarding her empty room. This was already a bit strange. Recently, I received a telegram from Los Angeles that Fairbanks and Pickford are negotiating a divorce! And Fairbanks' house on Pevirely Hills is also being put up for sale.

As for the clues to Fairbanks and Pickford's divorce, they can be recounted as follows. The Los Angeles telegram stated that Pickford's own reason for the divorce was incompatibility, and there was no other reason. Before this statement was made, Fairbanks and Pickford had already separated a few years ago. The first time Fairbanks went to Europe, he said it was for a business vacation. He later came to the East, and after being unknown for a long time, he made a hunting movie. He left his wife in Hollywood, saying that Pickford did not like to travel.

The second time, he and his son, Douglas Fairbanks Jr., went to London again. At that time, Douglas Fairbanks Jr. had just divorced Joan Crawford. He said it was a vacation and travel, and again said that Pickford did not like to travel. But Pickford had indeed traveled to England and Italy several times. Fairbanks said in Shanghai last time that he wanted to make a movie with Pickford in Shanghai. If the divorce is successful, this matter will inevitably become a bubble.

Fairbanks and Pickford were married in 1920. At that time, Pickford was 26 years old. When she married Fairbanks, she had just divorced Owen Moore. The reason for her divorce from Owen Moore was that he had abandoned her on their honeymoon, leaving for three days and then returning. Pickford recently inherited a £200,000 legacy from her mother's will.

Film Review of "Husband's Secret" 207

— Ling He

(A Paramount Production)

On such a hot summer day, going into the cool, air-conditioned Grand Theater to see such a delicate and sweet film, I think everyone must feel very satisfied. If we don't want to gain any new enlightenment or lessons from this film, then from the standpoint of entertainment, this kind of film can give people a feeling of relaxation and pleasure. And this view is not completely without social basis. I think the people who can leisurely walk into the Grand Theater, their original purpose is to enjoy themselves to the fullest.

At the same time, the main target audience for the production of such films is the highly educated Ladies and Centieman, so they strive for perfection in form. Anyway, this kind of audience will never be like the illiterate people who are excluded from the walls of the art palace, and they are unfathomable about the colorful European and American films. So in this sense, the author of "Husband's Secret" is very worthy of the appreciation of some audiences for being so exaggerated in his performance.

The director's technique is lively and compact, which is something that no one can ignore. For example, a group of swindling gamblers take a huge sum of money, and each of them puts on a tall hat and gets into the car, shaking hands and saying goodbye. Then the black curtain is uncovered, and its skillful technique unfolds the consistent light and fluttering mood of the future here. Furthermore, the protagonist sneaks away to a small town to pursue a woman who has not experienced the world. Although there are inevitable "coincidences" in the story, the performance of this love affair is very interesting and does not stick to the old ways. In particular, the fortune-telling with money to get engaged and the sketches in the car after the marriage are all extremely simple scenes. However, this long process is narrated in a very compact and clear manner. Perhaps these are not things that ordinary people can understand, but they are precisely the cleverness of the director. There are many similar scenes, such as the wife handing the bedroom key to the husband, such as the wife deliberately causing the husband to lose money, etc. Especially at the end, when the husband returns home from prison, the husband lies, the wife knows everything, and the matter ends there, which is even lighter. However, it is said that there are many more things later, but they are completely omitted from the film. In addition to the above, several main actors such as Clark Gable and Carole Lombard are just right. Dorothy McKail, who starred in "Red Passion and Green Meaning", only plays an unimportant supporting role here, but it is not a success.

What should be said again should be the content. As mentioned earlier, the content is very empty, and they are only working very hard on the form. However, we cannot ignore that the author is a very law-abiding artist, so the person with bad character is finally influenced by his wife and his conscience is discovered, and he voluntarily requests punishment. Precisely because of this, this is a fantasy that is 108,000 miles away from reality, so his preaching task is very clearly expressed.

Review of "Red Passion and Green Meaning" 208

— Wan Shi

This film is another ordinary production from Columbia.

Regardless of who is acting here, no one has the power to appeal. Even in terms of the acting skills of this film, they are almost all mediocre and vulgar. They can neither surpass the crowd nor are they very stagnant and rigid. The so-called "Doctrine of the Mean" is considered to have produced one more film. However, the two male and female protagonists are indeed acting sincerely, which is more commendable.

However, the failure of the entire play is definitely not just due to insufficient performance. The play itself has no value in existence. Of course, love tricks have already made people tired, let alone this love is a mediocre fabrication. For example, if the author wants to write about the greed of rich people for women, he can only monotonously describe him using money to buy love. At the same time, he promotes love above all else on the front, so the wealthy girl who is good at socializing terminates the contract with the rich man and elopes with the poor aviator. In this way, not only is there a significant contradiction in the behavior of the wealthy girl who gambles as much as she wants, but also this emphasis on the development of love makes the aviator's painstaking efforts in scientific research take a secondary position, and even just an accompaniment to the progress of love. As for the seduction of the aviator's sister, it is even more of an unimportant insertion. Although this is a more real life.

Since it is a plain and empty content, naturally there will not be amazing results in form. Although the director still has success in small places, such as writing about the night of intimacy of the couple, only focusing on the hats and skirts, and the (OK) on the flight and the car, they are all clever. The entire performance, of course, has a fairly clear narration, but this is only as clear and smooth as a primary school student writing an essay. As for the beginning, development, turn, and conclusion of the article, they are rarely used here. Therefore, a vulgar story finally gives people a vulgar impression due to the vulgar performance. After watching this film, I can only write this little opinion. In this way, the permission may not be sufficient, but such a movie can only teach people to write such superficial articles.

My Opinion on "The New Robin Hood" 209

— Confused

"The New Robin Hood" is entirely a story of foreign seven swords and thirteen heroes. The son of the Spanish Grand Duke, Genkham Muratay, uses his very erratic actions, very magical disguise, and fights against the three thugs who destroyed his family. Finally, the thugs kill each other by mistake and die. The consciousness of this film is that it does not need to be criticized, it is just the fantasy of the petty bourgeoisie.

As for the technical aspects, the director seems to want to make the development of the story as erratic as possible, and this is quite achieved.

In terms of actors, the performance of the male protagonist is also very erratic. This is the assimilation of the actor and the character in the play. Even if there is a good director, this kind of place cannot be achieved by an ordinary actor, especially the magnificence of the physique and the heroic posture, which are very suitable for the conditions of a strong man. But the most successful thing about "The New Robin Hood" is "disguise". Genkham Muratay appears several times in the play, and there is not a single appearance and appearance that is the same. What is particularly exciting is the twitching of the "black shadow". Because there is a wonderful snake in the grass here. When the audience sees the black shadow, they know that Genkham Muratay is coming. So wait nervously. I remember that Tarzan of the Apes had Tarzan's long roar as a clue, and "The New Robin Hood" used the black shadow as a clue, which was extremely successful.

Naturally, "The New Robin Hood" also has unreasonable places, that is, Colonel Reich does not investigate Genkham's behavior! Xu Genkham and his beloved daughter got married for no reason, because Reich had offered a reward to capture Genkham!

A Broken Bone Creates a Star 210

— Luo Fen

Marlene Hawkins' position was created by her broken bone. Maybe some people will find it strange, but this thing is real.

When Marlene Hawkins was a child, she accidentally broke her ankle bone at school. Later, after treatment, her ankle bone returned to its original shape. Later, she graduated and studied singing and dancing. She went to New York to perform dance skills in a dance hall on Broadway. Once, because she was too careless, her old broken ankle bone broke again. This time the doctor told her that she could no longer dance. After she recovered, she gave up her dancing career and engaged in drama. Later, she entered the film industry, and since then she has gradually become a movie star. Isn't her success as a star caused by her ankle bone?

The Moral Code of Movie Stars 211

— Ye Xingxing

No one has violated it in eleven years. In 1922, the giants of various film companies gathered and decided to include the "Moral Cause" in each contract.

The occurrence of this clause is green to the RoscoeFattyArbukle rape and murder case in San Francisco at that time. Although Albukie was acquitted, the American Women's Club banned him from sending the screen again. In order to prevent similar cases from happening in the future, the film company strictly set rules. If an actor commits an act that harms the reputation of the silver screen, the company can immediately cancel his contract. No one has committed this "moral code" for eleven years. One point is that it is worth praising the various companies. They cited this rule, regardless of gender, regardless of big stars and small roles, they treat them equally. Even Greta Garbo's contract has such a clause. Finally, someone discovered that Jack Koppel's contract did not use this clause. Try to imagine Koppel's young age, does he need this clause?

Anne Harding and George Arliss hesitated. They are afraid that the company will not trust their noble character, so they are hesitant to move forward. As a result, the "moral code" that the company has contracted has been reduced. After Anne Harding and Harry Bnmister got married, people called her a good woman from Hollywood. As for Arliss, she is old and virtuous, and is an extraordinary person. Then, why should the company do this? Of course, stars without shortcomings do not like to have such sentences in their contracts, and they do not like the kind of unnecessary opinions in the company. They may even quit because of it. They admit that in order to achieve even the smallest things, they are willing to sacrifice excellent contracts.

Movie Novel: The Irish Girl, Part 8 212

— One Hand

The second morning, during breakfast at the Ziggesters' house, everyone had different thoughts, except for Alaric, who was still able to eat. Mrs. Ziggister grumbled that Pang was truly ungrateful, now disregarding the grace of education and packing her clothes to leave. Alaric interjected, mocking his mother, saying that the so-called grace of education was only for the sake of two thousand pounds a year. Mrs. Ziggister, seeing that her son had exposed her true intentions, scolded him severely.

Childe came in, and everyone welcomed him. He bent down to kiss Isesseil. Seeing her haggard appearance, he asked what was wrong. Ziggister grumbled, revealing Pang's dishonorable act of being in Kmios's room last night. Childe firmly refused to believe such a thing, and seeing Pang approach, he went to meet her, wanting her to deny it. Isesseil couldn't help but reveal her mother's dark secrets, saying that her mother educated Pang only for the sake of two thousand pounds a year. Pang looked at them in turn with a strange expression, realizing that their kindness towards her was all for money!

Pang said in a low voice that she was going home, and they would just have to forgive her for the loss of one thousand pounds. Childe now felt he could no longer hide the truth from Pang and told her that her father was still at home, and what was said before was just a lie. Pang was truly overjoyed, shocked that the only confidant she thought she had would also deceive her for money, and happy that her truly beloved father was still alive. Pang cried out that she couldn't bear it anymore and rushed out the door.

Seeing this situation, Isesseil also felt she could no longer bear it and told Childe how her mother had coveted Pang's inheritance and did not hesitate to make her children do deceitful things. She further told him how her mother used Kress's love and how she planned to elope with him last night, and how Pang wanted to protect her. Childe's heart was in turmoil, and he left there in a daze.

After Pang returned home, the reunion with her family brought her the joy of family, but also a different kind of longing. Although she was dissatisfied with Childe's deceptive behavior, she could never forget him. One day, on her birthday, many friends came to the village to celebrate. She was already a young woman, how could she dismiss the feelings of longing for her lover? Her father led her to the [illegible character] and told her to close her eyes and sit and wait. At that time, the new moon was rising, and the moonlight shone on her tear-stained face. Footsteps approached her, she opened her eyes, she saw her beloved in front of her, she thought it was an illusion, closed her eyes and opened them again, it was indeed him! Childe hugged her again and said, "I love you"!
